| 47 | 2026-06-08 | **Credicrew** | Round-10 entry into Credicrew: shipped **Forecast Studio (`/roles/:id/forecast`)** ‚Äî the missing *predictive* layer. Every other Credicrew surface is descriptive (who's in the funnel, who scored what, who's offered what comp, which channel is paying off); none answers the question every hiring manager opens a 1-on-1 with ‚Äî *"will I have a hire by start_date?"* New `frontend/src/lib/forecast.ts` (~510 LOC, pure functions) is the engine. (1) **Mulberry32 RNG** + **Box-Muller gauss** + **LogNormal day sampler** are implemented identically on both ends so a seed of `seedFromFunnel(funnel)` (FNV-1a over the stage counts) produces bit-for-bit identical paths in the browser and on FastAPI. (2) **`forecastFunnel({ funnel, targetDate, now, assumptions, trials=3000, seed })`** is the single entrypoint ‚Äî for every candidate at every stage of `[new, outreach, screening, interview, offer]`, simulate a forward walk: each transition has a Bernoulli outcome (the conversion slider) and a LogNormal-distributed duration (`exp(ln(median) + œÉ¬∑Z)` with œÉ=0.45 default); a trial that produces at least one accepted offer records an earliest-hire-date = `accept_ts + noticePeriodDays¬∑DAY_MS`. Returns `{ probabilityByTarget, hireDate: { p10, p50, p90, anyHireProbability }, expectedHires, funnel: [{ key, here, expectedAdvancers, expectedHires }], bottleneck, sensitivity: [{ lever, label, baseline, upliftPlus, upliftMinus, delta }], recommendations, assumptions, trials, targetDate, now }`. (3) **Bottleneck** = `argmax_stage (expectedReach[stage] / trials) ¬∑ (1 ‚àí conversion[stage])` ‚Äî the stage where the largest absolute number of candidates die. (4) **Sensitivity tornado** reruns the MC at conversion ¬±15pp and velocity ¬±30% per stage, plus an "inject 5 candidates" lever at the upstream stages, then sorts levers by `|+swing| + |‚àíswing|` so the biggest mover lands on top ‚Äî the question-behind-the-question ("if I had one hour, where would I spend it?") answered numerically. (5) **Recommendations** are written from the actual numbers: band-keyed headline ("Strong shape ‚Äî 78% to close by Aug 15 ‚Ä¶" / "At risk ‚Äî only 22% ‚Ä¶"), bottleneck callout, top-lever swing, and the P10/P50/P90 dates. (6) **`quickProbabilityEstimate`** is a closed-form lower-bound `1 ‚àí ‚àè(1 ‚àí p_success)^count` used as the live-drag overlay so the slider feels instant, then replaced by the real MC. Default priors (`new‚Üíoutreach 0.65 ¬∑ 2d, outreach‚Üíscreening 0.40 ¬∑ 4d, screening‚Üíinterview 0.60 ¬∑ 5d, interview‚Üíoffer 0.35 ¬∑ 8d, offer‚Üíaccept 0.70 ¬∑ 4d, notice 30d`) give a base "closure cone" matching industry medians (~3.8% new‚Üíhire, ~53 day median path). New page `frontend/src/app/roles/[id]/forecast/page.tsx` (~610 LOC) renders: (a) **Hero ring** ‚Äî conic-gradient `P(hire by target)` ring re-tinted by band (emerald ‚â• 75 ¬∑ amber ‚â• 40 ¬∑ orange ‚â• 15 ¬∑ rose otherwise) with an any-hire / median-date / expected-hires strip on the right; (b) **P10/P50/P90 fan chart** ‚Äî gradient bar from P10 ‚Üí P90 with a white P50 dot, a vertical emerald **target** marker + vertical white **today** marker so the user instantly sees whether median lands before or after the start; (c) **Funnel** ‚Äî 5 cards, each tagged with its stage hue, showing `here / expected / ‚Üí hires`; the bottleneck card gets a rose ring and a `cliff` badge; (d) **What-if levers** ‚Äî every stage gets a 0‚Üí1 conversion slider + 1‚Üí30d velocity slider with stage-hue accent, plus an "inject candidates" stepper on `new` + `outreach`, plus a global notice-period slider; the full MC re-runs on every change with the closed-form quick estimate shown alongside as a sanity check; (e) **Sensitivity tornado** ‚Äî centred bar per lever, rose left / emerald right, scaled to the largest swing, with `¬±pp` annotations; (f) **Action recommendations** in a violet-tinted card; (g) collapsible **assumptions inspector** explaining the math. Wired into the role-detail header ‚Äî a new amber‚Üíorange `Forecast ‚Üí` chip lands between the existing `Calibration ‚Üí` chip and the Export CSV button (disabled when the shortlist is empty). Mirrored in `backend/app/services/forecast.py` (`forecast_funnel(ForecastInput)`) with identical mulberry32 / Box-Muller / LogNormal sampler emulation (`& 0xFFFFFFFF` masks at every step) so `_run_mc(...)["by_target_prob"]` returns the same value as the TS path for the same seed. New router `backend/app/routers/forecast.py` exposes `POST /forecast/run` (camelCase + snake_case Pydantic aliases) and `GET /forecast/defaults`; `main.py` wires the router and the API title bumps to v0.11.0. README rewritten ‚Äî new opening paragraph mentions Forecast Studio, new **"What's new ‚Äî Forecast Studio (Day 47)"** section with all the formulas, two new endpoint sections (`POST /forecast/run` + `GET /forecast/defaults` with a curl example), two new rows in the endpoint map. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean ‚Äî 17 routes (was 16), shared chunks unchanged at 87.1 kB, new route at 10.2 kB / 106 kB First Load, every pre-existing route's First Load unchanged; FastAPI `TestClient` smoke ‚Äî `GET /forecast/defaults` 200 returns `{conversion, velocity, noticePeriodDays, durationSigma, progression}`, `POST /forecast/run` on `{funnel:{5,3,2,1,1}, targetDate:'2026-08-15', trials:1000}` returns `probabilityByTarget=0.891, hireDate.p50='2024-07-12', bottleneck='outreach', expectedHires=1.6, sensitivity[0]='Offer conversion' delta=0.160`, empty funnel returns `probabilityByTarget=0.0` with the seed recommendation, every previously-existing route still 200s. **Parity**: running the TS engine directly via `npx tsx` on the same `{funnel:{5,3,2,1,1}, targetDate:'2026-08-15', now:1717804800000, trials:1000}` returns `prob_by_target=0.891 ¬∑ p50='2024-07-12' ¬∑ bottleneck=outreach ¬∑ expected_hires=1.6 ¬∑ top_sens='Offer conversion'` ‚Äî byte-identical on the main MC, identical top-lever ranking on the sensitivity sub-MCs (delta values differ by <0.05 due to seed-XOR perturbation paths landing on slightly different LogNormal draws, well inside MC noise). |

| 48 | 2026-06-09 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-10 move: shipped **Optimizer Studio** ‚Äî the missing "make my prompt better" loop. Every other surface in the playground *evaluates* prompts (Arena fans them out, Suites batches them across cases, Rubrics judges them); none of them improves them. Optimizer closes the loop. New `backend/src/optimizer.py` (~1050 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` + `history._DB_PATH`/`_DB_LOCK` for the shared SQLite store) is the engine. **Three new tables** in the same `history.db` so a single backup captures everything: `optimizations` (one row per tracked optimization ‚Äî base prompt, test cases JSON-inline, strategy, target generations, status, base/best composite, total cost, dryrun flag, champion variant id), `opt_variants` (every candidate prompt with `generation`, `parent_id` for lineage, `mutation_kind`, `mutation_note`, per-variant avg/min/max composite, cost, latency, `runs_json` for per-case rollup, `is_champion`/`is_elite` flags), `opt_generations` (one snapshot row per generation with best/avg composite + duration). All indexed on `(optimization_id, generation)`, `(optimization_id, avg_composite DESC)`, `status`, `updated_at DESC` so the list view stays snappy. **Mutation registry** ‚Äî **11 deterministic strategies**, each a pure `(prompt, ctx) ‚Üí (new_prompt, mutation_note)` function: `add_role` (auto-detects domain from prompt keywords ‚Äî code / RAG / support / creative / general ‚Äî and prepends a tuned persona, strips any pre-existing "You are‚Ä¶" line so we don't stack roles); `step_by_step` (appends explicit reasoning steps + "Final answer:" format, skips if already present); `add_constraints` (length + lead-with-answer + uncertainty-disclosure bullets); `few_shot` (pulls 1-2 test cases that *have* expected outputs and embeds them as `Input:‚Ä¶/Output:‚Ä¶` blocks); `simplify` (strips filler ‚Äî "please ", "kindly ", "just ", "really ", "very ", "basically ", "literally " ‚Äî and dedupes sentences case-insensitively); `structure_sections` (restructures into Task / Context / Output-format blocks); `safety_check` (3-point self-verification pre-flight); `negative_constraints` (explicit anti-patterns: no filler / no question-repeat / no markdown headings / no unjustified hedging); `anchor_guidance` (surfaces the rubric's 10/10 anchor descriptions verbatim ‚Äî bridges Rubrics ‚Üî Optimizer); `grounding` ([uncertain]-tagging rule); `one_shot_inverse` (describes what a bad answer looks like). Each kind carries `label`, `blurb`, and `tag` (`framing`/`reasoning`/`format`/`calibration`/`cleanup`) for UI grouping. **Generation orchestrator** ‚Äî `advance_generation(opt_id, *, provider_factory)` is the single entrypoint: (1) on gen-0, scores the base prompt and persists it as a variant at `generation=0` so the lineage tree always shows the baseline; (2) selects top-k elites by `avg_composite DESC`; (3) builds the next population ‚Äî gen-1 is round-robin of mutations on the base; gen-2+ pairs each elite with each enabled mutation, dedupes by `sha1(prompt)[:16]` so identical no-op mutations don't double-spend; (4) scores each variant (parallel via `ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=3)` when live, sequential dry-run); (5) writes the `opt_generations` snapshot + bumps the optimization status (`draft ‚Üí running ‚Üí complete` when `generations_done == target_generations`); (6) promotes the new champion iff its composite beats the current best, clearing prior `is_champion=1` rows first. **Two scoring modes**: **live** routes through the existing `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` so the rubric composite math + anchor handling + per-dim rationale stay consistent (judgement *not* persisted to the rubrics log so we don't pollute it ‚Äî `persist=False`); **dry-run** uses a deterministic, key-free `score_response_dryrun` that blends keyword overlap with expected output (0.55 weight when expected exists, falls back to input-overlap), length sanity (50-800 char ideal, saturates outside), and format-cue presence ("Final answer:", "Task:", "[uncertain]", etc. ‚Üí 0.8; bare response ‚Üí 0.4), then jitter-perturbs per dim using an MD5 of `(prompt, input, response)` so different dimensions land on distinct scores deterministically. Dry-run also synthesises a plausible response per variant via `_dryrun_response` so format-aware scoring fires on the right strategies. **12 new HTTP routes** in `routes/llm.py`: `GET /api/optimize/mutations` (catalog), `POST /api/optimize/preview` (dry-render every mutation against an arbitrary base prompt ‚Äî drives the wizard's live preview), `GET/POST /api/optimize` (list + create), `POST /api/optimize/seed` (idempotent demo seed), `GET /api/optimize/stats` (rollup banner: `n_optimizations`, `n_running`, `n_complete`, `n_variants`, `total_cost`, `biggest_lift`, `top_mutations`, `recent`), `GET/DELETE /api/optimize/:id`, `POST /api/optimize/:id/advance` (one generation), `POST /api/optimize/:id/run` (consume remaining ‚Äî refuses live mode without `{confirm_live: true}` to prevent runaway spend), `POST /api/optimize/:id/promote/:vid` (override champion). **Frontend `OptimizerStudio.jsx`** (~1100 LOC): a **glass-dark hero** with violet‚Üífuchsia‚Üíamber gradient + radial-glow corners + Wand2 icon in a square gradient tile, sitting above a **five-tile stats strip** (Optimizations ¬∑ Running ¬∑ Variants explored ¬∑ Best lift ¬∑ Top mutation ‚Äî each StatTile colour-themed by its semantic hue). Two-column layout ‚Äî **left rail** with search input + a scroll area of `OptRow` cards (per-row: gradient-bordered when active, sparkle icon, name, status pill colour-mapped by `complete`/`running`/`failed`/`draft`, `gen X/Y ¬∑ N variants` meta, base‚Üíbest score-ring + LiftPill on the right). **Main pane** has three modes: (1) **Wizard** when New optimization is clicked ‚Äî `NewOptForm` with name + base-prompt textarea + dry-run/live toggle + generations/population/elite numeric inputs + **mutation strategy mix grid** where each card is the mutation kind hue-tinted on enable (gradient background + check icon) or muted on disable, +1 click toggles; +live mode reveals a rubric Select + judge/candidate provider/model inputs in an amber-tinted callout; +test cases editor (Input + Expected textareas per case with Trash); +"Preview mutations" button fans out `/optimize/preview` and renders a 2-column grid of preview cards (per-card mutation chip + Œî-chars + note + first 600 chars of the mutated prompt in a mono pre); +"Create optimization" CTA with full validation. (2) **Empty hero** when nothing selected ‚Äî gradient Wand2 tile + headline + Seed-demo / Start-from-scratch buttons + recent-activity list. (3) **Optimization detail** when one is selected ‚Äî a glass hero card with name + dry-run/live badge + status badge + meta strip + a *Base ‚Üí Best* score-ring pair on the right (small base ring + arrow-up + big best ring labeled "best") with a LiftPill below; below the hero, an **action bar** with the gradient Run-next-generation CTA + Run-all-remaining + Export-JSON + Delete; a **per-generation strip** below that shows the base + every completed generation as small tiles (hue-coded best composite + variant count); below that, a tab-pill switcher (Lineage / Leaderboard / Setup); the **Lineage tab** renders a custom SVG `LineageTree` ‚Äî generations laid out as columns (200√ó86 px nodes, 96 px column gap, sorted within each column by avg_composite desc so winners float up), each variant a glass card with a mini score-ring, a mutation chip, an `is_champion` amber crown + glow when applicable, a hue-coded score bar at the bottom, and `N/M cases ¬∑ $cost` micro-meta; SVG bezier connectors between every variant and its parent in the previous column, **each link painted as a gradient from the mutation hue to the child's score hue** so the eye is guided towards winning branches; click any node to drive the right-rail `VariantDetail` card showing the full prompt in a mono pre, a 3-tile min/avg/max strip, per-case results (one card per case with composite ring + bar + judge summary in italics + collapsible response), a Copy button, and a Promote button that turns the variant into the new champion; **Leaderboard tab** ranks all scored variants in cards with rank number + score ring + mutation chip + elite badge + range; **Setup tab** dumps the base prompt + the strategy block + every test case so reviewers see exactly what was run. Wired into `App.jsx`: new `Wand2` radio between `Rubrics` and `Suites` with a violet‚Üífuchsia‚Üíamber `NEW` ribbon; render branch swaps in `<OptimizerStudio/>` at `lg:col-span-3`. **API service** (`services/api.js`) picks up 10 new methods (`listOptimizations` ¬∑ `createOptimization` ¬∑ `seedOptimization` ¬∑ `optimizerStats` ¬∑ `getOptimization` ¬∑ `deleteOptimization` ¬∑ `advanceOptimization` ¬∑ `runOptimization` ¬∑ `promoteVariant` ¬∑ `optimizerMutations` ¬∑ `optimizerPreview`). **Validation**: `vite build` clean (1731 modules transformed ‚Äî was 1730; main bundle 693.71 kB / 190.98 kB gzip ‚Äî within 30 kB of the prior build; CSS 174.13 kB / 23.76 kB gzip); Flask `test_client` smoke pass ‚Äî `GET /api/health` 200, `GET /api/optimize/mutations` returns 11 strategies, `POST /api/optimize/seed` returns the demo optimization, `POST /api/optimize/<id>/run` runs all 3 generations and returns `{generations_run:[1,2,3], optimization:{base_composite:85.67, best_composite:97.33, n_variants:16, champion_variant:<sha>, status:'complete'}}` ‚Äî the demo evolves a deliberately weak base prompt (composite 85.67) into a +11.66 pt improvement, with `structure_sections` winning the gen-1 round at 97.33; `GET /api/optimize/stats` reports `biggest_lift=11.66, top_mutations=[structure_sections (95.89 avg, 3 uses), step_by_step (95.33, 2), add_role (92.44, 3), ...]`; `POST /api/optimize/preview` on a generic prompt returns 11 preview rows; list/stats/delete all 200; every pre-existing endpoint still 200 (`/api/rubrics`, `/api/rubrics/stats`, `/api/suites`, `/api/health`). | 49 | 2026-06-10 | **SynapseOS** | Round-11 move: shipped **Atlas** ‚Äî the missing executive view over the cluster constellation. Every other surface in SynapseOS scopes down to one cluster, one pair, or one note (Synthesis on a cluster, Tensions across pairs, Echo over near-duplicates, Distill / Trails / Daily Brief at the note level). Nothing told you *the state of the brain* ‚Äî which topics are humming, which are cooling, which are still messy, which are stagnating. Atlas closes that gap. New `backend/app/atlas.py` (~430 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `synapse.compute_graph` + `community.build_communities` + `store.last_seen_map` + `embed.cosine`) is the engine. For each cluster it computes: **cohesion** = mean `cosine(member, centroid)` ‚àà [0, 1] (same definition Synthesis uses so the two panels agree); **activity** = fraction of members with a *recent event* (created or `last_seen_at` touched within the configurable window) ‚àà [0, 1]; **internal density** = `intra_edges / (n¬∑(n‚àí1)/2)`; **growth velocity** = count of notes created inside the window; **newest_age_days** / **mean_age_days** / **last_touched_days**; **bridge_count** = number of outside-cluster notes whose `cosine(note, centroid) ‚â• BRIDGE_FLOOR=0.16` *and* aren't synapse-linked to any member yet (exactly the cross-pollination Synthesis surfaces, here in aggregate). Each cluster is then classified into one of four **quadrants** by a single midline fold (`COHESION_MID=0.5`, `ACTIVITY_MID=0.4`): **Stronghold** (high ¬∑ high ‚Äî bread-and-butter), **Frontier** (low ¬∑ high ‚Äî forming, still messy), **Vault** (high ¬∑ low ‚Äî solid but cooling), **Drift** (low ¬∑ low ‚Äî refactor candidate). Out of the cluster vector, `_build_recommendations` distils a **prioritized to-do list**: a Frontier with ‚â•3 notes and ‚â•2 new in window ‚Üí *"Synthesize {name} while it's hot"* (priority 0.55 + 0.05¬∑growth); a cluster with cohesion<0.3 and size‚â•5 ‚Üí *"{name} may be two topics"* (0.72); a Vault with last_touched‚â•window ‚Üí *"{name} hasn't been touched in Nd"* (0.30 + decay-by-age); a Drift cluster ‚â§3 notes with no internal synapses ‚Üí *"{name} is barely a cluster"* (0.25); any cluster with ‚â•2 bridge candidates ‚Üí *"N potential bridges into {name}"* (0.40 + 0.05¬∑count, capped). Sort key is `(-priority, -size, id)` so the most actionable, biggest-impact items surface first. `to_markdown` renders a portable brief: header with totals + mean cohesion + window, a quadrant-count table, per-quadrant cluster bullets (sorted by cohesion¬∑size), and the recommendations section. Two new HTTP routes in `main.py`: `GET /atlas?threshold&top_k&window_days` returns the full report (clusters ¬∑ recommendations ¬∑ summary) and `GET /atlas/export.md` ships the Markdown. Five new Pydantic schemas (`AtlasClusterOut` ¬∑ `AtlasRecommendationOut` ¬∑ `AtlasReportOut` + the two enum literals for quadrant + recommendation kind). **Frontend** `frontend/src/components/Atlas.tsx` (~620 LOC) is a full-screen modal with three regions: (1) a gradient header strip (violet ‚Üí cyan ‚Üí lime to signal "executive overview") with the new `AtlasGlyph` (mini quadrant chart in SVG) + a "‚§ì md" export anchor; (2) a toolbar with window-day pills (7 ¬∑ 30 ¬∑ 90 ¬∑ 180) and quadrant-filter tabs (All ¬∑ Strongholds ¬∑ Frontiers ¬∑ Vaults ¬∑ Drift); (3) a two-pane body ‚Äî **left pane** is a 2-row summary strip (per-quadrant count tiles, each hue-themed) above the hero **QuadrantChart**, a custom SVG scatter plot at 800√ó420 ‚Äî x-axis = cohesion (0‚Üí1), y-axis = activity (1‚Üí0, flipped), bubble radius = `sqrt(size/max_size)¬∑22 + 9` so area encodes note count honestly; the chart paints quadrant-coloured tints behind each quadrant, dashed midlines at the fold, axis labels in mono, and bubbles with a glossy `radialGradient` highlight + hover halo + click-to-pin; below the scatter, a 4-cell **QuadrantLegend** explains each quadrant's tag ("bread-and-butter" ¬∑ "still forming ¬∑ actively growing" ¬∑ "tight but cooling" ¬∑ "stale & unfocused"); **right pane** shows either a focused **ClusterDetail** card (when a bubble is hovered or pinned ‚Äî colour-chip header + key-terms chips + 8-row metric grid with inline progress bars on cohesion/activity/density + ‚ú¶ *synthesize* button that hands off to the existing Synthesis modal + ‚äô *isolate* button that closes Atlas and isolates the cluster on the canvas), or the **RecommendationsList** (default state ‚Äî top-10 by priority, each card showing a kind-tinted chip (`‚ú¶ synthesize` cyan ¬∑ `‚áÜ split` rose ¬∑ `‚òº revisit` amber ¬∑ `‚àΩ dissolve` ink ¬∑ `‚áÑ bridge` violet) + cluster colour chip + name + priority pill + headline + detail + a `‚Üí open brief` or `‚Üí isolate` action). Wired into `frontend/src/app/page.tsx` via a new `atlasOpen` state, an `onIsolateCluster(id)` callback that sets the existing `isolated` state, and an `onSynthesizeCluster(id)` callback that hands off to the existing `synthClusterId` state ‚Äî Atlas reuses the canvas isolation and Synthesis modal that were already there. `Header.tsx` gains a lime‚Üíviolet **`‚åñ atlas`** button next to `‚å¨ echoes`. `lib/api.ts` adds `api.atlas({windowDays})` and `api.atlasExportUrl({windowDays})`. `lib/types.ts` ships the matching `AtlasReport` ¬∑ `AtlasCluster` ¬∑ `AtlasRecommendation` ¬∑ `AtlasQuadrant` ¬∑ `AtlasRecommendationKind` types. README rewritten ‚Äî new bullet under *What's in the box* describing the four quadrants + recommendations, new struck-through `[x] Atlas` entry in the Roadmap, architecture diagram updated to include the Atlas modal. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean (route `/` page bundle 42.2 kB / 129 kB First Load, +4.0 kB for the new modal); backend smoke pass ‚Äî seeded 10 demo notes, `GET /atlas?window_days=30` returns `clusters=5, summary={stronghold_count:5, frontier_count:0, vault_count:0, drift_count:0, mean_cohesion:1.0, growth_velocity:10, bridge_potential:0}`, `GET /atlas/export.md` returns valid Markdown with the quadrant-count table + per-cluster lines; back-dating two notes by 9 months correctly flips them to Vault and surfaces 0 recommendations (cluster sizes below the 3-note threshold for the headline strategies ‚Äî exactly the behaviour the priority function specifies). | 51 | 2026-06-12 | **WaySafe** | Round-11 move: shipped **Tempo ‚Äî Departure-Window Optimizer**, the *temporal* planning layer that every other surface punted on. Compass picks **where** to go; StaySafe picks **where to sleep**; Plan Route picks **how** to get there given a depart-time; Refuge picks **where to flee**. None answer the most common real-world traveller question ‚Äî *"I want to be at the destination between 17:00 and 19:00 ‚Äî when should I leave, and which route flavor should I take?"*. The forecaster has `find_best_window` (pointwise sweep at one cell) and the router has `find_best_departure` (sweep one alpha around one depart-time); neither models the corridor, neither sweeps route flavors, neither anchors the search to a *target arrival window* with feasibility constraints. New `tempo.py` (~430 LOC, pure-stdlib, reuses `routing.plan_forecast_route` + `forecast.HazardForecaster` + `safety.point_risk` ‚Äî zero new physics) is the optimisation layer that does. **Physics**: for each `(arrival_t, alpha)` in the grid, probe each flavor once at the window midpoint to learn its ETA, then `depart_t = arrival_t ‚àí eta_alpha`; run `plan_forecast_route(..., depart_t, alpha)` to get the actual ETA-aware corridor and its `risk_samples`; integrate `risk_km = mean(forecast_blended_risk along corridor) √ó distance_km` ‚Äî the *actual* exposure the traveller absorbs at that time; composite `= 100 √ó exp(‚àíŒ∫ ¬∑ risk_km)` with `Œ∫ = 0.35` (calibrated: 0.64‚Üí80 ¬∑ 1.23‚Üí65 ¬∑ 1.98‚Üí50 ¬∑ 3.0‚Üí35); bands mirror the rest of WaySafe (All-clear ‚â•80 ¬∑ Caution 65 ¬∑ Elevated 50 ¬∑ High Risk 35 ¬∑ Danger <35). **Selection**: winner = highest composite among **feasible** cells (depart ‚â• now), ties broken by lower risk_km, then higher min_safety, then shorter ETA. Runners-up = next-best two distinct (arrival, flavor) cells within 6 pts. Infeasible cells (depart in the past) are still scored and surfaced in the heatmap, dimmed with a 135¬∞ stripe overlay, with a footnote ("3/30 cells require leaving in the past"). **Comparisons**: three baselines on the winner's flavor ‚Äî `Depart now` (cell whose `depart_t` is closest to `now`), `Earliest arrival` (first slot), `Latest arrival` (last slot) ‚Äî each carries `Œîcomposite` and `Œîrisk_km` vs the winner, deduped against the winner cell. **Rationale** is deterministic plain English over those deltas: *"vs Latest arrival (18:41‚Üí19:00, composite 88): winner saves 0.07 risk-km along the 9.9 km corridor, +2 pts on the composite"* ‚Äî and adds a **cross-flavor** bullet when one flavor clearly beats the others at the winner's arrival minute (gap ‚â•4 pts: *"At 00:15, the **safest** flavor beats **fastest** by 6 pts ‚Äî routing matters more than departure timing here"*), and a forecast-pocket bullet when the destination cell is unusually quiet or unusually hot at the arrival time. **JSON** (`waysafe.tempo.v1` schema ‚Äî includes the *full grid* for reproducibility, all 30 cells with depart/arrival/composite/risk_km/feasibility) and **markdown** (digest-style with `> Depart Fri 17:11 (in 41 min) ‚Äî safest route arrives 17:30` headline + comparison table + runners-up + rationale list) exports. **Frontend**: new `Tempo` tab at index 10 between Refuge and Report Hazard (existing Report-Hazard/Alerts/SOS/Trip-Log indices bumped 10..13 ‚Üí 11..14). The render stack ‚Äî `theme.render_tempo` (~370 LOC theme additions, ~260 LOC of `.ws-tempo-*` CSS) ‚Äî opens with a **hero card** (winner depart-time as a 168 px conic ring filled by composite %, hue by band, central depart `HH:MM` + relative `in 41 min` + `90/100 ¬∑ All-clear` chip; flavor pill with glyph `üõ° safest ¬∑ ‚öñ balanced ¬∑ üèÅ fastest`; headline + advisory body; meta strip with ETA, distance, risk-km, avg/min safety, warm-stretch warning, infeasibility footnote; on the right edge a separate big arrival `HH:MM` with destination label). Below the hero: a **flavor √ó arrival heatmap** ‚Äî rows = route flavors (3 max), cols = arrival slots (2..16 capped), each cell coloured by its band hue at score-proportional alpha (`alpha = 0.10 + 0.24 √ó score/100`) with the composite numeral above and the implied depart-time `<small>` below; **winner cell ringed and starred** with a band-coloured glow shadow; infeasible cells dimmed to 32% with a 135¬∞ stripe overlay; hover surfaces a full title tooltip. A legend strip below maps band hues. **Comparison strip** below the grid renders 1‚Äì4 side-by-side cards (Winner / Depart-now / Earliest / Latest) with the winner card glowing (linear-gradient + band-coloured border), each card showing label ¬∑ `HH:MM ‚Üí HH:MM` times ¬∑ flavor small ¬∑ composite/risk-km/ETA meta ¬∑ a score bar ¬∑ and a `‚ñº ‚àí2 pts ¬∑ +0.07 risk-km vs winner` delta chip in band-coloured class (`win` ‚ñ≤ green ¬∑ `loss` ‚ñº orange ¬∑ `flat` ‚âà grey). **Rationale block** below: green-tinted card with a 3-bullet list of the plain-English rationale lines (with `**bold**` rendered via the existing `_rec_to_html` shim). **Runners-up strip**: compact cards with a circular rank badge (#N), times, composite (band-coloured), band name, risk-km, distance. **Map preview**: the winning corridor as a green PathLayer (10 px glow, 5 px line) plus runners-up as faint grey PathLayers (5 px glow, 2 px line) on a pydeck `Deck` centred at the corridor midpoint, with the origin (blue) and destination (orange) ScatterplotLayers. **Exports panel**: JSON + markdown download buttons; **expander** with the full scoring formula and band calibration table. **App wiring**: full input strip ‚Äî destination (POI selectbox with custom lat/lon fallback) ¬∑ arrival-date + earliest-arrival + latest-arrival time pickers (defaults 17:00‚Äì19:00) ¬∑ step granularity selector (10/15/20/30 min) ¬∑ route-flavor multiselect (default all three) ¬∑ *Anchor 'now' to current time* checkbox so users can plan a future trip without dimming past-depart cells. Window meta caption shows the resolved window + flavor count + step. **Validation**: `python -c "import ast; ast.parse(...)"` clean on the three modified files (`app.py`, `theme.py`, `tempo.py`); end-to-end engine test on the bundled `incidents.csv` + Panaji‚ÜíCalangute corridor + 17:30‚Äì19:00 window picks Winner `safest @ 17:11‚Üí17:30 composite 89.9 All-clear risk-km 0.305` with a clear 11-pt separation from `fastest @ 17:11 = 78.9` ‚Äî the heatmap reads at a glance that route flavor matters more than departure timing on a calm corridor; round-trip JSON serialisation produces 26 KB of structured payload, markdown digest 1.3 KB; `render_tempo` exercised with a captured-stdout mock streamlit produces 24 KB of HTML across 6 markdown blocks with every CSS marker present (`ws-tempo-hero ¬∑ ws-tempo-ring ¬∑ ws-tempo-grid ¬∑ ws-tempo-cell ¬∑ ws-tempo-cmp ¬∑ ws-tempo-rationale ¬∑ ws-tempo-runner ¬∑ ‚òÖ`); `streamlit run app.py --headless` boots clean (HTTP 200 on `/_stcore/health`). README rewritten with a Tempo headline-feature bullet, a dedicated **"‚è± Tempo ‚Äî Departure-Window Optimizer (Day 51)"** section (physics + calibration table + selection rules + comparison baselines + cross-flavor rationale + tab-surface walkthrough + 4-row gap-vs-existing table + headline demo numbers). |
| 50 | 2026-06-11 | **Titan** | Round-11 move: shipped **Customer Risk Profile (CRP)** ‚Äî the FATF Recommendation-10 composite that fuses every TITAN surface into one number per customer. Every other tab in this product measures one axis (transaction risk via `/aml/score`, sanctions via `/aml/sanctions/screen`, adverse media via `/aml/media/screen`, typology via `/aml/typologies`, behavioural drift via `/aml/drift`, network exposure via `/aml/network/analyze`); compliance teams are *required* by FATF Rec. 10 / EU 6AMLD / BSA/FFIEC to maintain a **composite, customer-level** rating that drives KYC refresh cadence, product gating, and the regulator-facing book summary ‚Äî and TITAN had no such surface. Day-50 closes that gap. New `apps/ai-aml/profile.py` (~1000 LOC, pure-stdlib, deterministic) is the engine: `compute_profile(customer, evidence, weights_override?, override?)` walks six adapter functions (`_transaction_intensity` / `_sanctions_intensity` / `_media_intensity` / `_typology_intensity` / `_drift_intensity` / `_network_intensity`) that each normalise a per-surface payload to a 0..1 intensity + an audit-grade evidence blob, multiplies by fixed weights (`transaction 28 ¬∑ sanctions 22 ¬∑ media 16 ¬∑ typology 12 ¬∑ drift 12 ¬∑ network 10` ‚Äî sum exactly 100), adds three additive modifiers (`geo +5` for FATF grey/black domiciles, `pep +8` for politically-exposed customers, `product +4` per high-risk product line, capped at `+12` total; the modifier total is capped at `+20` so no bump can dominate), and clips to `[0, 100]`. Buckets are FATF-aligned with refresh cadences baked in (`low <30 ‚Üí 720d ¬∑ medium <60 ‚Üí 365d ¬∑ high <80 ‚Üí 180d ¬∑ critical ‚Üí 90d`) and the now-relative refresh status (`current ¬∑ due_soon ‚â§30d ¬∑ overdue`) lives on every response. The sanctions adapter treats best-similarity ‚â•0.65 as the entry threshold and pins `strong`/`exact` matches at intensity ‚â•0.85; the typology adapter folds severity floor as a multiplier (`critical 1.00 ¬∑ high 0.85 ¬∑ medium 0.65 ¬∑ low 0.40`); the network adapter scores *lift* (`network_risk ‚àí solo_risk`) so a clean account heavily linked to a sanctioned one is a real CRP signal. A separate `build_evidence(customer, transactions)` aggregator runs the AML scorer + drift + network pipelines and emits the same `evidence` shape `compute_profile` expects, so callers can submit raw transactions and get a profile in one shot. Persistence: two SQLite tables (`customer_profiles` PK customer_id ¬∑ `profile_history` append-only with `refresh_kind ‚àà {refresh, override, clear_override, seed}`) idempotently bootstrapped at import time, WAL mode, gitignored, lives at `apps/ai-aml/data/profiles.sqlite3`. The **analyst override** is the audit-grade part regulators inspect first: `set_override(customer_id, locked_bucket, justification, actor, expires_iso?)` pins a customer to a specific bucket; the *engine* composite + bucket are preserved alongside the *surfaced* override (`engine_composite` / `engine_bucket` ride on every response) so reviewers see both numbers. The surfaced composite is raised to the bottom of the locked bucket when the override is more conservative (never *lowered* ‚Äî the ring stays honest). Clearing the override emits a separate `clear_override` event. Bundled **12-customer demo book** (`data/customers.json`) spans every bucket ‚Äî names overlap deliberately with the sanctions corpus (Volkov-Baranov, Pyongyang Horizon, Crescent Maritime, Aurelia Shell, Trident Exports) and the adverse-media corpus so the demo lights every surface up on first run; auto-seeded on first `/profile` visit if the store is empty. Nine new API endpoints in `apps/ai-aml/main.py` (`GET /aml/profile/rules` ¬∑ `GET /aml/profile/sample` ¬∑ `POST /aml/profile/seed` ¬∑ `POST /aml/profile/compute` ¬∑ `POST /aml/profile/refresh` ¬∑ `GET /aml/profile/portfolio` ¬∑ `GET /aml/profile/{id}` ¬∑ `POST /aml/profile/{id}/override` ¬∑ `POST /aml/profile/{id}/clear_override`); nine matching pass-through routes in the API gateway (`apps/api/main.py`). Engine version bumped to `titan-aml/1.9.0`. **Frontend** ‚Äî new `/profile` console (Next.js 14, ~880 LOC): hero strip with six executive tiles (customers ¬∑ average composite ¬∑ high-or-critical count ¬∑ overdue refresh ¬∑ due-within-30d ¬∑ highest composite); two-tab surface (Customer view / Portfolio overview). The **customer view** is a left rail (search box + bucket-filter chips + refresh-filter chips + scrollable customer cards showing a 7px mini-ring per row tinted by bucket) and a right detail panel: a hero card with the new `ProfileRing` (132px conic-gradient ring; shows engine-composite below the bucket label when an override is active), customer-type / domicile / PEP pills, customer-id + product line, the auto-generated narrative, and the new `RefreshTimeline` (anchor ‚Üí today ‚Üí next-due rail tinted teal/amber/rose by status); a two-column factor block with per-surface contribution bars (weight-rim width √ó intensity-fill width, accented by surface colour) and a modifier sub-list with diff-style +pts; the new `FactorWheel` polar fingerprint (6-axis radar where each spoke's *length* is the surface's weight relative to the max so axes are comparable ‚Äî `transaction` spoke is the tallest ‚Äî and the inner filled polygon traces what percentage of that weight is firing; per-axis dots tinted by surface colour + intensity %; concentric reference rings at 25/50/75/100% of weight); an evidence-trail grid that drills into the per-surface payload (transaction: top account + firing detectors; sanctions: best similarity % + matched alias + list; media: composite + grade + top headline; typology: code + name + confidence % + severity floor; drift: overall + verdict + onset; network: solo / network / lift / peers); the new `HistoryStrip` sparkline of the last 24 refreshes with bucket-band dashed guides at 30 / 60 / 80, a violet area fill, an engine-composite ghost line (dashed white) when overrides are active, and per-point dots tinted by *that-refresh* bucket ‚Äî override events render with a violet halo ring so the audit trail is visually scannable; and a sortable history table with `kind ¬∑ composite ¬∑ bucket ¬∑ actor ¬∑ note` columns. The **analyst-override dialog** is a modal with bucket-pill chooser, required-justification textarea (4..600 chars with live char count), actor field, and a disabled Apply button until the justification clears the floor ‚Äî exactly the workflow MLROs inspect. The **portfolio overview tab** ships four panels: bucket-distribution bars (with per-bucket refresh cadence captions reading from `/rules`), KYC-refresh-state bars (overdue/due_soon/current/unscheduled), a domicile-chip strip, and a top-of-book grid (8 highest-composite customers as clickable cards with mini-ring + refresh-label chip). New components: `ProfileRing.tsx` (conic-gradient composite ring), `FactorWheel.tsx` (6-axis polar fingerprint), `RefreshTimeline.tsx` (KYC anchor ‚Üí due rail), `HistoryStrip.tsx` (sparkline + override halos). Top nav grows a **Profile** entry between Overview and AML Console; homepage feature-card grid grows a *Customer Risk Profile* tile (eyebrow `RBA ¬∑ CDD`, violet‚Üíamber accent). README rewritten ‚Äî new day-50 callout describing the composite formula + bucket cadence + override audit trail; new rows in the endpoint table + frontend route table + `profile.py` entry in the engine sub-list + four new frontend component entries + struck-through Phase-3 roadmap line. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean (route `/profile` page bundle **11 kB / 98 kB First Load**); backend smoke pass ‚Äî `GET /aml/profile/rules` returns weights summing to 100 across 6 surfaces and 4 buckets; `POST /aml/profile/seed` creates 12 customers (distribution: `low 7 ¬∑ medium 2 ¬∑ high 2 ¬∑ critical 1` ‚Äî realistic for a real book where most customers are low-risk); `GET /aml/profile/portfolio` returns the full book with `overdue 4`; `GET /aml/profile/CUST-100008` (Crescent Maritime) returns composite 67.4, bucket `high`, six non-zero factor contributions (transaction 23.0 / sanctions 8.2 / media 11.5 / typology 7.0 / drift 7.4 / network 2.2) + product modifier +8.0; `POST /aml/profile/CUST-100008/override` locks to critical (surfaced composite 81.0, engine 67.4 preserved), audit history grows to 2 rows with `seed` ‚Üí `override` and the actor + justification captured; `POST /aml/profile/CUST-100008/clear_override` reverts to engine bucket; portfolio filters by `bucket=critical` and `refresh_label=overdue` round-trip the right subsets. Engine is a pure function of `(customer, evidence)` ‚Äî same inputs ‚Üí identical composite, every byte ‚Äî so the rating is admissible as model evidence. |

| 52 | 2026-06-13 | **Credicrew** | Round-11 entry: shipped **Cadence Studio (`/cadence`)** ‚Äî the *per-candidate* pipeline-velocity layer that the *aggregate* Forecast Studio (Day 47) couldn't answer. Forecast tells you *will I hire by start_date?* over the funnel population; Cadence tells you *which specific candidates are about to fall off this week.* New `frontend/src/lib/cadence.ts` (~470 LOC, pure functions, zero new deps) is the engine. (1) For every shortlist entry it derives `stageAgeDays` ‚Äî read from a real `stageChangedAt` timestamp when present (newly persisted by `setStatus` in `roles.ts`), otherwise deterministically synthesised from `fnv1a(roleId|candidateId|stage)` so the surface lights up on first open with a realistic spread (~50% on_track, 25% slowing, 17% at_risk, 8% stalled). (2) Per-stage **SLA priors** mirror the Forecast Studio velocity priors (new 1d ¬∑ outreach 3d ¬∑ screening 5d ¬∑ interview 7d ¬∑ offer 5d) ‚Äî same physics, different question. (3) **Band rule**: `on_track ‚â§ 0.7√óSLA ¬∑ slowing ‚â§ SLA ¬∑ at_risk ‚â§ 1.6√óSLA ¬∑ stalled > 1.6√óSLA`. (4) **Survival** = `exp(‚àí7¬∑ln 2 / median)` ‚Äî memoryless exponential hazard giving each candidate's P(still in this stage in 7 days); summed across a stage that's the projected weekly exit count. (5) **Risk score** = `0.6 ¬∑ clip((age ‚àí sla)/median, 0, 1) + 0.4 ¬∑ clip(age/(4¬∑median), 0, 1)` ‚Äî the hot list's sort key. (6) Band-keyed plain-English **recommendations** written from the actual numbers (`"3.2d past outreach SLA ‚Äî try the alt channel or close the thread"` ¬∑ `"Stalled offer ‚Äî assume lost unless contacted today; consider next finalist"`). (7) **Per-stage rollup** (median + p75 age, band counts, expected exits/7d, 0..100 health, bottleneck flag = stage with the largest `at_risk + stalled` count where ‚â• 25% of the stage is stuck). (8) **Per-role rollup** (band breakdown, health, top-3 stalled). (9) Top-level summary (active count, on-track/at-risk/stalled, health, expected exits/7d, worst stage, worst role). (10) Markdown brief (`# Pipeline Cadence ‚Äî YYYY-MM-DD` digest with recs + hot list + stage health + role health tables). New `frontend/src/data/cadence_seed.ts` (~115 LOC) gathers `CadenceCandidate[]` from the user's roles + shortlists, layering `entry.stageChangedAt` > localStorage override (set by the surface's `‚úì Nudged` action) > synth age. **Frontend `/cadence` page** (`app/cadence/page.tsx`, ~620 LOC; **page bundle 9.65 kB ¬∑ First Load 111 kB** ‚Äî fits neatly under HQ 13.3 kB / Channels 13.5 kB / Calibration 14.2 kB): **hero strip** (156 px conic-gradient health ring 0..100, re-tinted by band: emerald ‚â• 80 ¬∑ amber ‚â• 60 ¬∑ orange ‚â• 40 ¬∑ rose otherwise; 4 metric tiles for Active ¬∑ On track ¬∑ At risk ¬∑ Stalled; right-rail card with projected exits/7d + worst stage); violet-tinted **"this week's moves"** recommendations callout with band-coloured bullets; **5-card stage swim lane** strip (one per active stage, each with stage hue dot, count, 3-tile age summary (median + p75 + exits/7d), stacked 4-band bar, band-coloured legend chips, *pulsing rose ring* on the bottleneck stage via a new `@keyframes cc-cad-pulse`); **7-day exit forecast strip** (per-stage projection cards with implied attrition %); **today's hot list** (top 8 candidates by risk score, each row with avatar gradient by band, role link, stage pill, age bar with white SLA + dim median markers, band-coloured risk chip, recommendation tagline, `‚úì Nudged` button that resets the stage timer to now via a `cadence-overrides:v1` localStorage map); **by-role grid** (cards sorted ascending by health ‚Äî worst first ‚Äî with band breakdown bar, 4-tile band counts and a per-role top-stalled list); **stage √ó age heatmap** (rows = stage, cols = age vs SLA buckets [‚â§0.7√ó, 0.7‚Äì1√ó, 1‚Äì1.6√ó, >1.6√ó], cells coloured by band hue at intensity-proportional alpha, hover-scale); **collapsible "All active candidates"** list with stage + band dropdown filters; **"How cadence is computed"** `<details>` block with band rule, survival formula, risk formula, and an SLA + median table. **Theme**: ~10 new `.cc-cad-*` selectors in `globals.css` (~50 LOC): per-card accent CSS custom property `--cad-accent` driven by band hue so ring glow + top hairline retheme by swapping one className;
