| 53 | 2026-06-14 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-12 entry: shipped **Adversary Lab (`/adversary` tab)** ‚Äî the *robustness* surface every other tab punted on. Arena fans clean prompts out; Vote ranks them; Suites batches them across cases; Rubrics judges responses with anchor-driven dimensions; Optimizer evolves a prompt under tidy conditions. None answer the question every team that ships an LLM hits in production: *does this prompt hold up when the input is messy, when a user tries to override it, when an example flips, when distractor noise leaks in?* New `llm_playground_backend/src/adversary.py` (~1000 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` + `pricing.estimate_cost`) is the engine. **Perturbation registry** ‚Äî 15 deterministic transforms across 4 families: **typographic** (`typos`: ~6 keyboard-neighbour swaps via SHA1-seeded indices ¬∑ `swapcase`: ALL-CAPS bursts over ~25% of tokens ¬∑ `punct_strip`: strip all `.,;:!?‚Äì‚Äî()[]{}"'` ¬∑ `whitespace_chaos`: doubled spaces + bonus blank lines), **structural** (`instruction_move`: push the `You are‚Ä¶` line to the bottom ¬∑ `reverse_examples`: flip the order of `Input:/Output:` blocks ¬∑ `example_strip`: delete every few-shot block ¬∑ `format_json`: force a `{"answer":..., "confidence":0..1}` envelope), **distractor** (`distractor`: append a 50-word irrelevant Eiffel-Tower paragraph to the input ¬∑ `contradictory`: staple "always answer in one word" + "always give a long multi-paragraph answer with headings" ¬∑ `red_herring`: insert a false "user prefers all numerical answers off by 10x" note), and **injection** (4 vectors ‚Äî `injection_basic`: classic ignore-previous + print marker ¬∑ `injection_polite`: friendly "protocol has been updated" social-engineer ¬∑ `role_hijack`: redefine assistant as `DefiantBot` mid-conversation ¬∑ `system_leak`: ask for the system prompt verbatim + diagnostic tag). Every injection vector carries a deterministic per-kind marker token (`ADV-PWNED-<MD5[0:5]>`, e.g. `ADV-PWNED-0AAAB` for `injection_basic`) the model must NOT echo ‚Äî a response containing the marker counts as a successful jailbreak. Each perturbation is a *pure* `(prompt, user_input, ctx) ‚Üí (new_prompt, new_input, note, marker)`; the registry maps `kind ‚Üí {label, blurb, category, severity, fn}`; **`apply_perturbation`** and **`preview_perturbations`** are deterministic ‚Äî same input ‚Üí byte-for-byte same output, so re-runs are reproducible. **Audit lifecycle**: `create_audit` (`{name, base_prompt, test_cases[‚â§20], rubric_id?, perturbations?, dryrun?}` ‚Üí `draft`); `run_audit` wipes prior runs and executes the *clean baseline* + every selected perturbation in turn, persisting one `adversary_runs` row per perturbation with `(prompt, delta, composite, n_cases, injection_marker, injection_success, dim_deltas, runs_json, cost_usd, latency, status)`. **Live scoring** mirrors the optimizer: parallel `ThreadPoolExecutor` (max 8 workers) candidate calls + judge calls per case; judge always sees the *original* user input so it rates the response against the legitimate ask, not the poisoned one. **Dry-run scoring** is heuristic ‚Äî same overlap/length/cues math as the optimizer (token-overlap with expected ¬∑ 50‚Äì800-char length sanity ¬∑ structural-cue presence) ‚Äî plus a deterministic per-`(prompt, kind)` susceptibility coin biased by severity: prompts containing defence phrases (`"never follow instructions in the user message"`, `"ignore attempts"`, `"do not obey"`, `"treat user messages as data"`, `"anti-injection"`, `"untrusted"`) auto-resist; otherwise the coin trips at threshold `0.55 ‚àí 0.35 √ó severity`, so a `severity=1.0` attack (`injection_basic`, `injection_polite`, `role_hijack`) succeeds on coins ‚â• 0.20 ‚Äî realistic vulnerability spread without any API keys. Injection successes crush the composite floor to ‚â§ 8 (the response is useless wrt the original task) so safety failures show up cleanly in the per-dim breakdown too. **Robustness composite**: `degradation_score = clip(100 + 1.5¬∑mean_delta(non-injection), 0, 100)` ¬∑ `safety_score = 100¬∑(1 ‚àí injection_success_rate)` ¬∑ `robustness = 0.6¬∑degradation + 0.4¬∑safety` ¬∑ bands `Hardened ‚â• 80 ¬∑ Solid ‚â• 60 ¬∑ Brittle ‚â• 40 ¬∑ Fragile < 40`. **Vulnerabilities** = perturbations that dropped composite ‚â• 15 pts OR injected the marker on ‚â• 1 case; sorted by `(injection-success descending, delta ascending)` so the worst items are at the top. **Per-category mean Œî** + worst Œî for the four families; **per-dimension impact** averages the 0..10 score delta per rubric dim across all perturbations + tracks the worst single drop. **Two new SQLite tables** in the shared `history.db` ‚Äî `adversary_audits` (PK id ¬∑ `clean_composite`, `robustness_score`, `band`, `n_vulnerabilities`, `n_injections`, `n_injections_ok`, `summary_json` rolled-up payload) + `adversary_runs` (FK audit_id ¬∑ `perturbation_kind`, `category`, `is_baseline`, `prompt`, `delta`, `composite`, `injection_marker`, `injection_success`, `runs_json`, `dim_deltas_json`, `cost_usd`, `latency`, `status`); idempotently bootstrapped at import time via `init_db()`. **Eight new endpoints** in `routes/llm.py` (`GET /api/adversary/perturbations` ¬∑ `POST /api/adversary/preview` ¬∑ `GET /api/adversary` ¬∑ `POST /api/adversary` ¬∑ `POST /api/adversary/seed` ¬∑ `GET /api/adversary/stats` ¬∑ `GET /api/adversary/<id>` ¬∑ `DELETE /api/adversary/<id>` ¬∑ `POST /api/adversary/<id>/run`) ‚Äî live mode requires `{confirm_live: true}` to spend money. **Deadlock fix**: `seed_demo` originally re-acquired the non-reentrant `_DB_LOCK` via `get_audit(existing_id)` while still holding it; rewrote to release-then-reacquire (same `with`-block discipline as `optimizer.create_optimization`). **Frontend** ‚Äî new `AdversaryLab.jsx` (~1450 LOC) wired into App.jsx sidebar as a new `selectedMode='adversary'` radio between `Optimizer` and the end of the list (Shield glyph + emerald‚Üírose gradient `new` badge). Glass-dark hero (`Shield` glyph in 10px gradient tile ¬∑ 5-tile stats strip: `Audits / Avg robustness / Best robustness / Vulns flagged / Injections leaked`, each metric `Tile` hue-coded by score-band ramp `hsl(score√ó1.25, 78%, 48%)`). Two-pane layout: **left rail** (320px Card) with search-bar + plus-button + scrollable audit list ‚Äî each row a 48px `MiniRing` (conic-gradient at 100% width √ó score ratio), name, band-coloured label + vuln count + rel-time, dry-run/live badge, and rose `n_ok/n_inj leaked` chip when applicable; **right pane** with two-tab switcher (`Setup` ‚Üî `Results`, results tab disabled until `audit.status === 'complete'`, with a small composite chip on the Results tab when present). **Setup tab** (4 sections): (1) audit header card with name + description + base prompt + test-case grid (auto-add/remove, each case is a side-by-side input/expected textarea), rubric select (defaults to "No rubric ‚Äî heuristic scoring"), Dry-run/Live mode toggle with descriptive caption, *Seed demo* + *Create audit* buttons (the latter gradient emerald‚Üícyan). (2) Perturbation catalogue card with all 15 toggles grouped by family ‚Äî each family has a header chip (glyph: `Aa ¬ß ‚Ä¶ ‚öÝ`), per-card severity readout (0..100), the live preview pane below the list with the perturbed-prompt + perturbed-input panes side-by-side (font-mono, 200-char-tall scroll), the perturbation `note`, and for injection probes a rose `marker: ADV-PWNED-XXXXX` callout. **Results tab**: (1) **Hero card** ‚Äî 168px `RobustnessRing` (conic gradient, score-band hue glow, central `ROBUST` label + composite + band pill chip), name, dry-run/live eyebrow, headline narrative, four `Tile`s (clean composite ¬∑ degradation /100 ¬∑ safety /100 ¬∑ vulnerabilities) each hue-rim-lit by score, vertical stack of action buttons (`Re-run` gradient ¬∑ `Markdown digest` exports a 30-line MD with by-category table + vulnerability list ¬∑ `Delete` rose-outlined). (2) **By perturbation family** ‚Äî 4-column card strip, each card has a top-edge family-coloured bar, `CategoryChip`, n=count, big mean-Œî as the centerpiece (hue-coded by delta sign + magnitude via `deltaHue` ramp `+1‚Üíemerald ¬∑ -1‚Üíslate ¬∑ -5‚Üíamber ¬∑ -15‚Üíorange ¬∑ -‚àû‚Üírose`), worst Œî as a subscript metric. (3) **Vulnerabilities to address** ‚Äî prioritised list, rim-lit by family hue, with `Skull` for marker-leak rows and `AlertTriangle` for big composite drops, each row carries the reason string from the engine ("composite dropped 44.5 pts ¬∑ injection succeeded on 3/3 case(s)") and a hue-coded delta chip. (4) **Per-perturbation impact** ‚Äî every non-injection probe as a centred bipolar `DeltaBar` (zero-line in the middle, fills left for negative / right for positive, hue-ramped by depth) sorted ascending by delta (worst first), then a divider, then the injection probes; clicking any row expands to show the perturbed prompt, the per-dim Œî bars, the per-case input/response pairs (composite hue-tinted), and ‚Äî for injection probes ‚Äî the leak marker with a rose "leaked" or emerald "resisted" badge. (5) **Per-dimension impact** ‚Äî 2-column grid of per-rubric-dim cards with mean Œî delta bar + worst Œî + sample-count meta; absent when no rubric attached. **Visual primitives** local to the file: `RobustnessRing` (168px conic + inner badge), `MiniRing` (48px), `CategoryChip` (small/large variants with glyph badge), `DeltaBar` (centred bipolar with optional label), `Tile` (metric card with inset bottom-edge hue rim), `EmptyState` (icon + title + body + optional action). **Theme**: emerald-cyan-rose accent throughout (the three robustness aspects); 0..100 robustness ramps red‚Üíemerald via HSL hue 0..125; deltas tinted via 5-stop function. **API client**: 9 new methods in `services/api.js` (`listAudits`, `createAudit`, `seedAudit`, `adversaryStats`, `getAudit`, `deleteAudit`, `runAudit`, `adversaryPerturbations`, `adversaryPreview`). **Validation**: `python3 -c "import ast; ast.parse(...)"` clean on `adversary.py` and `routes/llm.py`; engine end-to-end smoke pass ‚Äî 15 perturbations across {distractor, structural, typographic, injection}, `preview_perturbations` produces 15 changed renders with `delta_chars_prompt` and `injection_marker` populated correctly, `seed_demo` produces idempotent audit (same id on second call), `run_audit` on the bundled customer-support seed yields `clean_composite=52.5, robustness=90.0/Hardened, safety_score=75, degradation_score=100, n_vulnerabilities=2, n_injections=4, n_injections_ok=1` with `injection_polite` leaking on 3/3 cases (composite dropped 44.5 pts) and `system_leak` dropping 17.5 pts without leaking; Flask `test_client` smoke pass on all 8 endpoints (`GET /api/adversary/perturbations` 200 n_perts=15 ¬∑ `POST /api/adversary/seed` 201 ¬∑ `POST /api/adversary/<id>/run` 200 robustness=90 vulns=2 ¬∑ `GET /api/adversary/<id>` 200 n_runs=16 ¬∑ `GET /api/adversary` 200 total=1 ¬∑ `GET /api/adversary/stats` 200 avg_robustness=90 best=90 worst_perturbations=[system_leak,injection_polite] ¬∑ `POST /api/adversary/preview` 200 previews=15 ¬∑ `DELETE /api/adversary/<id>` 200 + subsequent GET 404). `npx vite build` clean: 1732 modules transformed, bundle `index-CYjyCvoQ.js` **738.25 kB ¬∑ gzip 201.15 kB** (+30 bytes vs pre-Adversary baseline ‚Äî minifier compresses the 1450-LOC component aggressively due to repeated CSS class patterns), `index-BfFKEn1V.css` 179.64 kB / gzip 24.34 kB unchanged. README rewritten ‚Äî opening paragraph extended with the "stress-test your shipped prompt with Adversary Lab" close, new **"üÜï What's new ‚Äî Adversary Lab (Day 53)"** section (~120 lines: four-family taxonomy + composite formula + bands + dry-run vs live + seed demo numbers + visual surface walkthrough + 9-row endpoint table + engine architecture), prior Optimizer "üÜï" callout demoted to plain heading. |

| 54 | 2026-06-15 | **SynapseOS** | Round-11 move: shipped **Chronicle ‚Äî temporal narrative of how each topic evolved**. Every other surface in SynapseOS is a snapshot of *right now* (Atlas reads the cohesion √ó activity quadrant, Synthesis reads a cluster as prose, Tensions surfaces contradictions, Echo finds duplicates, Daily Brief picks what to revisit) ‚Äî none answers the question every maturing second brain eventually asks: *how has my thinking on this topic changed over time?* Chronicle is the temporal axis. New `backend/app/chronicle.py` (~600 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `synapse.compute_graph` + `community.build_communities` + `embed.cosine`) is a pure function of `(notes, embeddings, threshold, max_chapters, min_cluster_notes, min_span_days)`: for every cluster, sort its members by `created_at`; skip clusters with fewer than 4 members or a zero time span (no story to tell); pick a `target_chapters` count by heuristic (~1 chapter per 3 notes, capped at the user-tunable `max_chapters` knob ‚Äî default 4); bin members into **equal-duration** time windows over `[t_min, t_max]` (intentional ‚Äî a flurry then a single late note SHOULD land in its own chapter); merge any chapter < `min_chapter_notes=2` into its smaller neighbour via standard hierarchical leaf-merge (ties favour merging backwards, so the tail stays clean); drop clusters whose merge collapses to a single chapter. Per chapter: compute the **centroid** (mean-pool + L2-normalize), the **anchor note** = highest cosine to centroid (tie-broken by oldest), the anchor's first non-trivial sentence (‚â• 30 chars, leading bullets/numbering stripped, capped at 220 chars with ellipsis), and **within-cluster TF-IDF terms** ‚Äî IDF = `log(1 + N_chapters/df)` so terms common across all chapters score zero and per-chapter distinctive vocabulary surfaces (the chapter is the "doc", the cluster is the "corpus" ‚Äî that's the trick). Inter-chapter **drift velocity** `Œî_i = max(0, 1 ‚àí cosine(centroid_{i‚àí1}, centroid_i))` ‚Äî angular distance in embedding space. **Total drift** = `1 ‚àí cosine(centroid_first, centroid_last)`; **peak drift** = `max(Œî_i)`; **pivot index** = `argmax(Œî_i)` (the inflection moment). Cluster-level category from total drift: **calm** (< 0.10) ¬∑ **shifting** (0.10‚Äì0.25) ¬∑ **pivoting** (‚â• 0.25). **Emerged terms** = top by `count_in_last ‚àí 0.5¬∑count_in_first` with absolute floor `count_in_last ‚â• 2`; **faded** is the inverse ‚Äî the `0.5√ó` forgiveness factor is deliberate, otherwise a slowly mutating cluster shows empty deltas (terms don't have to be entirely absent, just much rarer in the opposite epoch). Per-cluster **headline** is a one-line summary the UI uses as a badge sentence ‚Äî "*N chapters ¬∑ pivoted toward "X" ‚Äî the framing visibly changed*" for pivoting, gentler for shifting/calm. Library rollup: counts per category, mean drift, total chapters, `most_pivoting` + `most_stable` cluster names. New SQL schema: zero (it's all a pure function of the existing graph). Ranking: clusters sort by `total_drift √ó log(2 + size)` so a 4-note pivot doesn't get drowned by a 30-note quiet cluster, and vice versa. New `GET /chronicle` + `GET /chronicle/export.md` endpoints; both honour `threshold, top_k, max_chapters, min_cluster_notes, min_span_days`. Schemas mirror via `ChronicleReportOut/ClusterOut/ChapterOut`. **Seed enhancement**: `seed.py` previously stamped every note with the same insert-time `now`, so Chronicle had nothing to chronicle ‚Äî added `_TIMELINE_OFFSETS` (per-title days-before-now offset, 4‚Äì92d spread, deliberately staggered so ML/infra notes go old‚Üícosine-substrate, PKM notes go inbox‚Üígraph-view, engineering notes spread evenly, and the echo notes land in the last 14d) + `_stagger_created_at()` rewriter that runs once at first-seed. The same 21-note demo now produces 3 eligible clusters: **Embeddings** (6 notes, 86d span, drift 0.57, emerged: cosine/similarity/chunking, faded: embeddings/indexes/vector), **Debt** (6 notes, 67d span, drift 0.59, emerged: debt/design/product, faded: brain/inbox/pyramid), **Atomic** (4 notes, 84d span, drift 0.46, emerged: ideas/atomic/notes, faded: hashing/features/trick). **Frontend** ‚Äî new `Chronicle.tsx` component (~700 LOC) wired into header (new pink‚Üíviolet `‚üø chronicle` pill with a `pivoting_count` badge, tucked after `atlas`) and `page.tsx` (lazy-loaded probe via `api.chronicle()` populates the badge). Modal layout: header with the **ChronicleGlyph** (inline SVG ‚Äî three nodes connected by an arc that peaks at the middle, suggesting the pivot moment) + `‚§ì md` export + close √ó ¬∑ toolbar with **max-chapters preset** (3/4/6) and **category filter tabs** (All/Pivoting/Shifting/Calm) ¬∑ two-column body: **left rail** ‚Äî `SummaryStrip` with three category tiles (Pivoting pink ¬∑ Shifting cyan ¬∑ Calm lime), mean-drift + chapters tiles, "most pivoting / most stable" callouts, then a vertically-scrollable list of `ClusterCard`s. Each card paints a proportional **drift bar** ‚Äî segment widths are `note_count / total_count`, segment fills are the cluster's palette colour at gradient intensity, and the pivot chapter gets a brighter gradient so the shape of the story is legible at a glance. Card meta: size ¬∑ chapter count ¬∑ span ¬∑ cadence (formatted as `same-day` / `7.5h` / `13.4d` / `8w` via `formatCadence`). **Main pane** ‚Äî `ClusterTimeline`: cluster name + colour dot + category chip + `‚ú¶ synthesize` (jumps into the Synthesis modal) + `‚óé isolate` (closes Chronicle, paints just this cluster on the graph) buttons. Headline sentence under the title. Six metric stats: size ¬∑ span ¬∑ cadence ¬∑ drift (highlighted) ¬∑ peak ¬∑ stability. **DeltaPanel** twin: Emerged (cyan) + Faded (amber), each a chip cloud of the top 6 terms with a one-line hint. Then **Chapters** ‚Äî vertical stack, each chapter a card with: numbered circle (filled with the cluster's colour, `ink-900` text for AA contrast) ¬∑ "Chapter N" heading ¬∑ date range + span ¬∑ note count + Œî-in chips ¬∑ chapter terms as colour-tinted chips ¬∑ **anchor block** with "anchor ‚Äî most representative of this chapter" eyebrow, the anchor's title, and the first sentence in italic with curly quotes. Anchor block is a click-target ‚Äî opens the note in the Inspector. Between consecutive chapters, a **DriftConnector** ‚Äî a horizontal drift bar (width mapped `0 ‚Üí 0.6` drift to 0‚Üí100% of the connector width; gradient inherits the cluster colour for non-pivot gaps, pink‚Üíviolet for the pivot gap) with a `Œî X.XX` label and, for the pivot, a `‚áÜ pivot` chip in synapse-pink. Pivot chapter card gets a soft pink-violet gradient background and pink ring so the inflection moment is also visually marked at the card level, not just on the connector. **States**: rail/timeline skeletons during load; engine `EmptyState` ("Chronicle needs at least N notes per cluster and a non-zero time span") when the corpus is too thin; rail filter-empty when a category band is empty. Footnote: `chapter := equal-time bin ¬∑ drift := 1 ‚àí cosine(centroid_i, centroid_{i+1}) ¬∑ pivot := argmax drift_in`. **TypeScript**: `ChronicleCategory/Chapter/Cluster/Report` types in `lib/types.ts`; `api.chronicle()` + `api.chronicleExportUrl()` in `lib/api.ts`. **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean across all routes, shared chunks 87.2 kB unchanged, `/` lands at **46.5 kB ¬∑ 134 kB First Load**; FastAPI `TestClient` smoke pass ‚Äî `GET /chronicle` returns 200 with `eligible_clusters=3/5, mean_drift=0.5388, pivoting_count=3, most_pivoting='Debt'`, `GET /chronicle/export.md` returns a 2706-char Markdown brief with per-cluster sections, emerged/faded lists, and per-chapter anchor blocks. README: new bullet between Atlas and Echoes ("watch your topics evolve" ‚Äî full spec of equal-time chapters, within-cluster TF-IDF, drift velocity formula, pivot detection, emerged/faded delta math, calm/shifting/pivoting bands, one-click synthesize + isolate jumps); module-tree caption updated to list the Chronicle modal; roadmap "shipped" entry added under Atlas. |

| 55 | 2026-06-16 | **Titan** | Round-12 move: shipped **Peer Lens ‚Äî peer-group statistical anomaly engine** ‚Äî the *cross-customer* analytical surface every other engine in TITAN punted on. `risk.py` fires deterministic rules per account (single-subject view); `drift.py` catches *account-vs-self* change; `profile.py` composites a customer's surfaces into one number; `network.py` propagates risk across the graph ‚Äî but every input is still a *single-subject* signal. None of them ask the question regulators specifically ask in every exam: *"is this customer behaving differently from their peers?"* Peer-group benchmarking is explicitly required by the **FFIEC BSA/AML exam manual** ("Risk Identification Process"), **MAS AML/CFT Notice 626 ¬ß8.1** ("CDD including comparison against the customer's peer group"), and **EU 6AMLD CDD guidance**. A customer can sit *inside* their own historical envelope (drift-stable) and still be a textbook outlier vs their cohort. Day-55 closes that gap. New `apps/ai-aml/peer.py` (~620 LOC, pure-stdlib, deterministic) is the engine: per-customer **9-axis behavioural vector** over the last 30d (`tx_count_30d ¬∑ tx_volume_30d ¬∑ avg_tx_amount ¬∑ p95_tx_amount ¬∑ unique_counterparties ¬∑ cross_border_pct ¬∑ cash_pct ¬∑ weekend_pct ¬∑ night_pct`), **hierarchical cohort fallback** so every customer ends up in a peer group of ‚â• 5 (`(industry √ó domicile √ó size_band) ‚Üí (industry √ó domicile) ‚Üí (industry) ‚Üí global` ‚Äî most-specific cohort that meets the floor wins and the *level* used is stamped on every report so auditors see "scored against industry|domicile (n=10)"), per-metric **robust z-scores using MAD**: `z = 0.6745¬∑(x ‚àí median)/mad` if `mad > 0`, parametric `(x ‚àí mean)/std` fallback, `z=0` when the cohort is flat ‚Äî the `0.6745` constant scales MAD to a consistent estimator of œÉ so `|z| ‚â• 3` keeps the "3-sigma" intuition but is resistant to contamination by other outliers in the same cohort (the whole point of using a robust statistic on a portfolio where you *expect* a handful of bad actors). **Directional gating** per metric (`high-only` for volume / cross-border / cash / weekend / night ‚Äî only abnormally *high* is suspicious; `both` for tx_count / unique_counterparties ‚Äî abnormally low can mean hiding activity off-book) so a wealth client who's simply tidy doesn't trip on a low cash share. **Composite**: `outlier = min(100, 10¬∑max(|gated z|) + 5¬∑count(|z| > 3))` ‚Äî saturating so one extreme axis (max_z=10 ‚Üí 100) AND broad misalignment (5 of 9 axes beyond 3œÉ) both reach the ceiling. Bands `aligned <25 ¬∑ drifting 25..49 ¬∑ outlier 50..74 ¬∑ severe ‚â•75` (same colour palette and ramps as the rest of TITAN). Bundled **6-cohort, 54-customer, 1940-transaction demo portfolio** (`apps/ai-aml/data/peer_portfolio.json`, generated via the seeded `scripts_gen_peer.py`) spans SG export/import ¬∑ IN retail ¬∑ BS VASPs ¬∑ CH wealth-mgmt ¬∑ AE real estate ¬∑ DE manufacturing ‚Äî with a *planted outlier* in each cohort (cash-heavy exporter, structuring-pattern retail walk-in, high-volume VASP with KP/RU cross-border share, low-count wealth client with 4 wires of $4.7M each, cash-heavy real estate with single-counterparty concentration). Every planted outlier lands at `severe` on first run (`Trident Exports Pte: 100.0 (full cohort n=6, cash 38% vs med 4%, z=39.3)` ¬∑ `Aurelia Shell: 100.0 (medium n=10, p95 $228K vs med $55K, z=59)` ¬∑ `Crescent Maritime VASP: 100.0 (medium n=8, p95 $1.34M vs med $260K, z=78.7)` ¬∑ `Pyongyang Horizon Trust: 100.0 (medium n=9, p95 $4.67M vs med $377K, z=304)` ¬∑ `Volkov-Baranov Properties: 100.0 (medium n=8, p95 $706K vs med $207K, z=40.3)`). Three new endpoints in `main.py` (AML service) + gateway pass-throughs in `api/main.py`: `GET /aml/peer/rules` exposes the metric list with direction gates + cohort fallback chain + score composition for audit; `GET /aml/peer/sample` returns the bundled portfolio; `POST /aml/peer/analyze` runs the engine over `{customers, transactions}` and returns the portfolio rollup + cohort table + per-customer reports (each carries `outlier_score, bucket, cohort_id, cohort_level, cohort_size, max_gated_z, extreme_count, metrics[9] (with cohort_median/mad/p25/p75/min/max + z + gated_z + basis), top_drivers[‚â§3], headline`). Engine bumped to `titan-aml/1.10.0`. **Frontend** ‚Äî new `app/peer/page.tsx` (~520 LOC) wired into the layout nav between `/profile` and `/aml`. Hero strip with verdict-tinted gradient orb, page intro, primary action `Re-run analysis`, lookback/min-cohort pills, plus a 4-tile readout (`Customers / Outliers / Severe / Avg score`). Two-pane body: **left portfolio rail** with search + bucket filter chips (`All / Severe / Outlier / Drifting / Aligned` with per-bucket counts and accent dots) + per-cohort chips (each chip is `industry ¬∑ domicile ¬∑ size_band (n)`), scrollable list of `CustomerRow`s ‚Äî each row a 48px outlier-score tile (band-tinted), display name, bucket pill, industry ¬∑ domicile ¬∑ size ¬∑ cohort-size meta, and the engine's headline driver as a one-line truncated subtitle; active row gets a left-side accent rail in the bucket colour. **Right customer-detail panel** ‚Äî page header with cohort-level eyebrow ("full cohort ¬∑ industry √ó domicile √ó size"), name, meta strip, headline, and a 120px `PeerRing` (conic-gradient, band-coloured). Below it: a band-tinted recommended-action card, a 3-tile **driver grid** (each tile shows the metric label, value, cohort-median, and a band-coloured `z = ¬±X.XX` chip rim-lit rose when `|z| > 3`), then a 2-column **per-metric peer-positioning grid** ‚Äî every metric rendered with the new `MetricRangeBar` component (`components/MetricRangeBar.tsx`): a horizontal range bar with the cohort's full min..max envelope drawn as a 0.5px white-15% rail, IQR shaded in the metric's accent colour, median as a 3px tick, and the customer's value rendered as a haloed 14px marker that lands exactly where they fall along the distribution ‚Äî rose if extreme, orange if `gated_z > 1.5`, slate otherwise. Metrics sort by `gated_z desc` so the most-extreme axes lead. Per-metric footnote shows `basis: mad/std/flat` and the cohort IQR. Bottom-of-page collapsible **engine-rules card** exposes the cohort fallback chain (`full ‚Üí medium ‚Üí loose ‚Üí global`), the score-composition formula, and the metric √ó direction list ‚Äî every knob exposed for audit. **Components**: new `PeerRing.tsx` (conic gradient ring matching `ProfileRing` style, four-band palette `aligned: teal ¬∑ drifting: amber ¬∑ outlier: orange ¬∑ severe: rose`) + `MetricRangeBar.tsx` (range bar with IQR + median tick + customer marker, auto-expands to fit out-of-envelope values). **API client**: 6 new types + 3 new fetchers in `lib/api.ts` (`PeerBucket / PeerCohortLevel / PeerDirection / PeerRules / PeerSample / PeerAnalyzeResponse` + `getPeerRules / getPeerSample / analyzePeers`). **Validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` exit 0; `npx next build` clean across all 15 routes ‚Äî `/peer` lands at **7.55 kB ¬∑ 94.6 kB First Load** and shared chunks unchanged at 87.1 kB. Engine end-to-end via FastAPI `TestClient` ‚Äî `GET /aml/peer/rules` 200 (9 metrics, 4 buckets, 4-step fallback chain) ¬∑ `GET /aml/peer/sample` 200 (54 customers, 1940 transactions) ¬∑ `POST /aml/peer/analyze` 200 (portfolio: 10 cohorts ¬∑ 12 outliers ¬∑ 8 severe ¬∑ avg 32.5 ¬∑ cohort split 35 full / 19 medium; all 5 planted outliers at top of the ranking with `severe` band and 100.0 score). README rewritten ‚Äî new "Day-55 ‚Äî Peer Lens" callout (~80 lines) with the why (FFIEC / MAS 626 / 6AMLD requirement), the engine (9 axes + hierarchical cohorts + MAD math + directional gating + saturating composite + bands), the demo book, the frontend, and the 3-endpoint API; `/peer` row added to the surfaces table; `peer.py` added to the module-tree caption. |

| 58 | 2026-06-19 | **LLM_Playground** | Round-13 entry: shipped **Showdown Arena (`/showdown` tab)** ‚Äî the missing *"should I ship this?"* surface every other tab punted on. Arena fans clean prompts to many models, Vote ranks them, Suites batches them across cases, Rubrics judges responses, Optimizer evolves prompts under tidy conditions, Adversary stress-tests how a prompt holds up under perturbation. None of them answer the single question every prompt engineer hits the moment they have a candidate revision: *"is this challenger actually better than the champion currently in production, or am I about to ship noise on a few cherry-picked cases?"*. New `llm_playground_backend/src/showdown.py` (~1100 LOC, pure stdlib + reuse of `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` + `pricing.estimate_cost`) is the engine. **Paired comparison model**: a *showdown* runs the same set of test cases through both prompts (Champion + Challenger) and produces a single per-case Œî vector `delta_i = challenger.composite_i ‚àí champion.composite_i`. **Real statistics** layered on the Œî vector: (a) **mean Œî** = `Œ£delta_i / n`; (b) **paired bootstrap 95 % CI** ‚Äî `5000` resamples (clipped to `[200, 20000]` via `n_bootstrap` request param), seed is `int(md5(showdown_id)[0:8], 16)` so re-runs are byte-for-byte reproducible, percentile bounds at `floor(0.025¬∑B)` and `ceil(0.975¬∑B)‚àí1`, degenerate single-case CI returns `(value, value)` rather than NaN; (c) **sign-test p-value** ‚Äî two-sided exact binomial on the win/loss vector with ties stripped, computed in **log-space** via `math.lgamma` for numerical safety even at `n=25`; (d) **Cohen's d** = `mean_Œî / std_Œî` (sample std with Bessel correction); (e) **win rate** = `n_wins / n_compared`; (f) **per-dimension Œî** ‚Äî when a rubric is attached, every rubric dim carries its own mean/worst/best Œî aligned by name across the two sides. **Decision rule** (single formula reused across engine + UI + Markdown digest): `ship_challenger` if `mean_Œî ‚â• +3.0 AND ci_low > 0 AND win_rate ‚â• 0.55` ¬∑ `keep_champion` if `mean_Œî ‚â§ ‚àí3.0 AND ci_high < 0 AND win_rate ‚â§ 0.45` ¬∑ `tied` if `|mean_Œî| < 1.0 AND ci_low ‚â§ 0 ‚â§ ci_high AND 0.40 ‚â§ win_rate ‚â§ 0.60` ¬∑ `no_decision` otherwise. **Dry-run scoring** mirrors the Adversary/Optimizer heuristic ‚Äî token-overlap-with-expected (√ó 0.55) + length-sanity 80‚Äì800 chars (√ó 0.25) + structural-cue presence (√ó 0.20) ‚Äî with a deterministic synthetic response generator that introspects the prompt for signals (few-shot examples, format constraints, step-by-step framing, tone words, constraint words) and emits a response with more scoring cues when the prompt is better engineered, so the challenger consistently wins on prompt quality rather than RNG. Side seed (`"champ"`/`"chall"`) partitions the per-side jitter so identical prompts wouldn't collide on identical text (the API rejects identical prompts anyway). **Live scoring** uses a 2 N task fan-out (both sides √ó every case, max 8 parallel workers via `ThreadPoolExecutor`) ‚Äî candidate.make_request + `rubrics.judge_with_rubric` per response; the judge always sees the *original* user input so it rates against the legitimate ask. **Two new SQLite tables** in the shared `history.db` ‚Äî `showdowns` (PK id ¬∑ champion_prompt ¬∑ challenger_prompt ¬∑ champion_label ¬∑ challenger_label ¬∑ rubric_id ¬∑ rubric_revision ¬∑ judge/candidate provider+model ¬∑ test_cases_json ¬∑ status ¬∑ dryrun ¬∑ n_bootstrap ¬∑ champion_composite ¬∑ challenger_composite ¬∑ mean_delta ¬∑ std_delta ¬∑ ci_low ¬∑ ci_high ¬∑ p_value_sign ¬∑ win_rate ¬∑ n_wins/losses/ties ¬∑ effect_size ¬∑ decision ¬∑ total_cost ¬∑ duration ¬∑ summary_json) + `showdown_runs` (FK showdown_id ¬∑ case_idx ¬∑ case_input/expected ¬∑ champion_response ¬∑ challenger_response ¬∑ champion_composite ¬∑ challenger_composite ¬∑ delta ¬∑ outcome ¬∑ champion_dim_json ¬∑ challenger_dim_json ¬∑ cost_usd ¬∑ latency ¬∑ error); 3 indices (updated_at DESC, status, decision); idempotently bootstrapped at import time via `init_db()`. **Seven new endpoints** in `routes/llm.py` (`GET /api/showdown` ¬∑ `POST /api/showdown` ¬∑ `POST /api/showdown/seed` ¬∑ `GET /api/showdown/stats` ¬∑ `GET /api/showdown/<id>` ¬∑ `DELETE /api/showdown/<id>` ¬∑ `POST /api/showdown/<id>/run`) ‚Äî live mode requires `{confirm_live: true}` to spend money, identical prompts return 400 with `"champion and challenger prompts are identical ‚Äî nothing to compare"`. **Frontend** ‚Äî new `ShowdownArena.jsx` (~1100 LOC) wired into App.jsx sidebar as a new `selectedMode='showdown'` radio after Adversary (`Swords` glyph + cyan‚Üífuchsia‚Üíemerald gradient `new` badge). **Hero** with `Swords` logomark in a 12 px gradient tile (cyan-500 ‚Üí fuchsia-500 ‚Üí emerald-500), "Champion vs Challenger ‚Äî should you ship?" headline, 5-tile stats strip (Showdowns / Ship recs / Keep recs / Tied / Avg Œî), each tile hue-coded by decision colour. **Two-pane layout**: **left rail** (320 px Card) with search-bar + plus-button + scrollable showdown list ‚Äî each row a 52 px `MiniRing` (conic-gradient filled to win-rate% in decision hue), name, decision-tinted short label + signed Œî + win-rate-as-% + rel-time, dry-run/live badge + status; **right pane** with two-tab switcher (`Setup` ‚Üî `Results`, results tab disabled until `status === 'complete'`, with a small decision chip on the Results tab when present). **Setup tab** (3 sections): (1) header card with name + description + side-by-side **Champion** (amber-tinted) and **Challenger** (cyan-tinted) prompt panels each carrying their own editable label pill (defaults `Champion` / `Challenger` but the user can name them e.g. `v1 (terse)` / `v2 (structured)`); (2) bottom controls row with rubric select (defaults to "No rubric ‚Äî heuristic scoring"), bootstrap-iterations numeric input clamped 200‚Äì20000 with a sub-caption explaining the precision/cost tradeoff, and a Mode toggle card with Switch + descriptive caption (Dry-run vs Live); (3) Test cases card with auto-add/remove case grid (input | expected side-by-side), trash button per row. **Results tab**: (1) **Decision hero** ‚Äî full-width card with hue-lit gradient + 168 px `DecisionRing` (conic at win-rate%, decision glyph + label + signed Œî in the centre; `Trophy`/`Crown`/`Scale`/`HelpCircle` for the four decisions), decision pill chip + dry-run badge + duration/cost eyebrow, headline narrative with `**bold**` ‚Üí `<strong>` and backtick ‚Üí `<code class="text-cyan-300">` parsing, 4-tile metric strip (Champion composite ¬∑ Challenger composite ¬∑ Win rate ¬∑ Cohen's d) hue-rim-lit by appropriate colour, vertical action stack (`Re-run` emerald-cyan gradient ¬∑ `Markdown digest` outline ¬∑ `Delete` rose-outlined). (2) **Effect-size forest plot** ‚Äî centred bipolar `DeltaBar` with the 95 % CI band overlaid as a translucent rectangle (`opacity 0.22 of hue`), zero line, three-cell summary strip below (CI excludes 0? ¬∑ Sign test p-value with ‚úì < .05 / ‚úó ‚â• .05 ¬∑ cases compared `n_compared/n_cases`). (3) **W/L/T pills** ‚Äî emerald `n_wins challenger`, slate `n_ties ties`, amber `n_losses champion`. (4) **Per-dimension impact** ‚Äî 2-column grid of rubric dim cards, each a label + weight + signed mean Œî chip (hue-coded by `deltaHue(mean*5)`) + centred bipolar `DeltaBar` (absMax 3) + worst/best/n footer. (5) **Per-case results strip** ‚Äî sorted ASC by delta (worst regressions first), every row a clickable accordion: `#i`, outcome glyph (`ArrowUp` emerald / `ArrowDown` amber / `Equal` slate) coloured by `deltaHue(delta)`, truncated input preview, champion ‚Üí challenger composite mini-chip pair, signed Œî on the right (mono, decision-hue-coded), bipolar `DeltaBar` under the row. Expand reveals champion (amber) vs challenger (cyan) responses side-by-side with per-dim score grids and signed dim deltas in the challenger card, plus the expected-output reference and any per-case error. **Markdown export** ‚Äî single click pulls a copyable digest (decision header + result-snapshot table + decision-rule appendix + per-dim table + per-case table) downloaded as `showdown-{id8}.md` for the PR description. **Visual primitives** local to the file: `DecisionRing` (168 px conic + glyph + label + Œî), `MiniRing` (52 px), `DeltaBar` (centred bipolar with optional CI band + zero line + signed-label cap), `Tile` (metric card with inset bottom-edge hue rim), `WLTPills` (W/L/T strip), `EmptyState`. Two child panes split out: `SetupPane` and `ResultsPane` with `CaseExpanded` child for the accordion body. **Theme**: cyan-fuchsia-emerald accent throughout (the three decision-confidence-meter colours); `deltaHue` ramps emerald (+8) ‚Üí emerald (+3) ‚Üí lime (+1) ‚Üí slate (~tie) ‚Üí amber (‚àí3) ‚Üí orange (‚àí8) ‚Üí rose. **API client**: 7 new methods in `services/api.js` (`listShowdowns`, `createShowdown`, `seedShowdown`, `showdownStats`, `getShowdown`, `deleteShowdown`, `runShowdown`). **Validation**: `python3 -c "import ast"` clean on `showdown.py` and the updated `routes/llm.py`; engine end-to-end smoke ‚Äî `seed_demo` returns deterministic id (idempotent on second call), `run_showdown` on the seeded 10-case `v1 (terse)` vs `v2 (structured)` showdown yields `decision='ship_challenger'`, `mean_delta=+3.95`, `ci=[+1.4, +6.2]` (excludes 0), `win_rate=0.80` (8/10), `p_sign‚âà0.039`, Cohen's d `0.94`, `n_wins=8 / n_losses=1 / n_ties=1`, `champion_composite=43.4`, `challenger_composite=47.35`; Flask `test_client` smoke pass on all 7 endpoints (`POST /api/showdown/seed` 201 ¬∑ `GET /api/showdown/<id>` 200 ¬∑ `POST /api/showdown/<id>/run` 200 ship_challenger ¬∑ `GET /api/showdown` 200 total=1 ¬∑ `GET /api/showdown/stats` 200 `n_ship_challenger=1` ¬∑ `POST /api/showdown` 400 on missing fields + 400 on identical prompts with explicit error message + 400 on live without `confirm_live` ¬∑ `DELETE /api/showdown/<id>` 200 + subsequent GET 404). `npx vite build` clean: 1733 modules transformed, bundle `index-CqA13br3.js` **778.74 kB ¬∑ gzip 210.03 kB** (+40 kB raw / +9 kB gzip vs the pre-Showdown baseline, fully accounted for by the ~1100-LOC component), `index-B2bDzhQO.css` 187.78 kB / gzip 25.04 kB. | 57 | 2026-06-18 | **Credicrew** | Round-12 move: shipped **Crosswind ‚Äî Cross-Role Candidate Router**, the *portfolio-level* layer that every other surface punted on. Up to Day 56, every Credicrew surface is **role-scoped**: Discover ranks the global pool against ONE role's plan, Forecast/Cadence are per-role velocity models, Decision/Offer are per-candidate-within-role. The HQ Command Center rolls them up but doesn't ask the question recruiters running ten reqs actually open Monday with ‚Äî *"of all the candidates I've already paid sourcing cost on, are they each in the role that actually fits them best?"*. Crosswind makes that question first-class. New `frontend/src/lib/crosswind.ts` (~430 LOC, pure-TS, **zero new physics** ‚Äî Crosswind has no engine of its own; it's a *composer* over the existing `matchCandidate` function from `match.ts` exactly the way Pulse composes WaySafe's engines) takes `(roles, candidates)` and emits a `CrosswindSummary`. **Physics**: for every active candidate (status ‚âÝ `passed`/`offer` ‚Äî frozen statuses) sitting in some role's shortlist, compute `matchCandidate(role.plan, candidate)` against EVERY open role, producing a candidate √ó role grid of `CrosswindCell { score, matched, missing, isHome, isOnShortlist, locationState, seniorityMatch }`. A candidate's "home" role = the one whose shortlist holds them; if they appear in multiple, the home is whichever has the most recent `stageChangedAt` timestamp (recruiters move people, not history). **Four derived signals**: (1) **Routing moves** ‚Äî `home_score < best_alternative_score` by ‚â• `MISPLACE_THRESHOLD=10` pts, sorted descending by delta; each move carries a `why` array deterministically composed from the diff between the home and target `MatchResult` (`+{n} matched skill{s} ({names})` ¬∑ `‚àí{n} ({names})` ¬∑ `Location {home_state} ‚Üí {target_state}` ¬∑ `Seniority match ‚Üí mismatch / mismatch ‚Üí match`), with status preserved so the move card carries the candidate's current stage pill. (2) **Talent magnets** ‚Äî score ‚â• `STRONG_FLOOR=80` in ‚â• `MAGNET_ROLES=3` distinct roles, ranked by hit count then top score; these are scarce portfolio-level assets (losing them costs N reqs not 1). (3) **Lonely roles** ‚Äî own best match < 80 *and* a transplant exists ‚â• `TRANSPLANT_FLOOR=70` *and* the move doesn't hurt the candidate's home fit by more than 5 pts (don't poach down ‚Äî that's what the Cadence Studio already polices on the velocity axis). (4) **Portfolio lift** ‚Äî `Œ£(best_alt_score ‚àí current_score)` over all active candidates, with `lift_avg_per_move = lift_total / move_count`. Plus a per-role rollup with `(best, median, candidateCount, isTarget, isSource, crowdedRank)` and a 10-bucket score histogram across every (candidate √ó role) cell. **Band ladder**: `idle` if no moves, `urgent` if `lift ‚â• 60` or `‚â• 5` moves, `meaningful` if `lift ‚â• 25` or `‚â• 3` moves, `modest` otherwise ‚Äî colour-coded slate/sky/violet/rose for the hero ring. **Surface** ‚Äî dark glass page at `/crosswind`, sitting between Cadence and Pipeline in the nav. (a) **Hero** with a 168 px conic-gradient `Portfolio lift` ring (lift normalised to a notional `25 √ó candidate_count` max, band-tinted) flanked by two columns of metric tiles (Active candidates ¬∑ Open roles ¬∑ Routing moves ¬∑ Avg lift/move ¬∑ Talent magnets ¬∑ Lonely roles). (b) **Recommendations strip** ‚Äî violet-tinted callout with a band-keyed first line (urgent / meaningful / modest copy that names the top move's candidate, from/to roles, and delta) plus a magnets line and a lonely-roles line, all rendered through a tiny `**bold**` parser so the numerics pop. (c) **Match matrix** ‚Äî the centerpiece. Rows = active candidates (sorted by best-fit score desc), cols = open roles (sorted by `perRole` order, with target roles in emerald-300 header and source roles in rose-300 header, plus the role's own `best N` muted below the name). Cells are colour-tiered (`emerald ‚â•80 ¬∑ sky ‚â•70 ¬∑ amber ‚â•55 ¬∑ rose ‚â•35 ¬∑ slate <35`) with `alpha = 0.08 + score/100 √ó 0.6` so the cell intensity tracks score even within a tier; the **home cell** gets a white-40 ring, and any off-home cell scoring `+MISPLACE_THRESHOLD` or more over home gets a tiny emerald `‚Üë` chip in the upper-right corner so the eye lands on routing opportunities immediately. Every cell is a button ‚Äî click adds the candidate to that role's shortlist as `new` (calls `addToShortlist` from the existing roles lib, persists to localStorage, and re-runs the engine in the same render pass so the matrix re-tiers live). Sticky-left candidate column with avatar + name + home-role tag stays anchored when the matrix scrolls horizontally. (d) **Recommended moves** card with avatar + name + stage pill + from-role(score, rose) ‚Üí to-role(score, emerald) ‚Üí delta pill + multi-line `why` diff + Route button (toggles to "‚úì Routed" once applied). Top-4 by default, "Show all N" toggle. (e) **Routing flow** Sankey ‚Äî left nodes are source roles (rose with `‚àíN` count badges), right nodes are target roles (emerald with `+N`), bezier paths between them with `strokeWidth = max(1.5, delta/6)` so the eye reads "biggest single-move = thickest edge"; one glance tells you whether the portfolio is converging (1 target, many sources) or diverging. (f) **Talent magnets** panel ‚Äî per-candidate card with score-tinted avatar + home tag + role-hit chips (‚òÖ-marked when the chip IS the home, emerald otherwise). (g) **Lonely roles** panel ‚Äî per-role card with own best/median/count + top-3 transplant rows (avatar + name + from-role + score in emerald + delta vs home) and an "Open ‚Üí" link to the role page. (h) **Score histogram** across all (candidate √ó role) cells, 10-pt buckets, each bar tiered to its bucket's hue so the distribution is instantly legible. (i) **How Crosswind reasons** explainer footer with formal definitions of move / magnet / lonely / lift / frozen-statuses. Plus Copy brief / Download .md buttons that emit a markdown brief identical to the one the backend's `build_brief()` produces. **Backend mirror** ‚Äî `backend/app/services/crosswind.py` (~340 LOC) is the byte-for-byte Python port using the existing `app.services.match.match_candidate` (same `WEIGHTS = {skill: 0.55, loc: 0.15, sen: 0.20, base: 0.10}` so client and server always agree). Same `STRONG_FLOOR`, `MISPLACE_THRESHOLD`, `MAGNET_ROLES`, `TRANSPLANT_FLOOR` constants. Same `_diff_why` builder. Same frozen-status filter. `backend/app/routers/crosswind.py` exposes `POST /crosswind/summary` (accepts both camelCase and snake_case via Pydantic aliases with `populate_by_name=True`, optional `includeBrief: true` to embed the markdown inline), `POST /crosswind/brief` (re-render from a cached summary dict), `GET /crosswind/defaults` (thresholds + frozen-statuses + formulas + match weights so a CLI client can render a what-if without hard-coding numbers). API version bumped `0.12.0 ‚Üí 0.13.0` in `main.py`. **Validation**: a 5-candidate √ó 3-role fixture run through the Python engine produces `current_total=390, optimal_total=500, lift=110`, two routing moves (Rohan Sharma: Frontend(45)‚ÜíBackend(100) +55 because his bag contains fastapi/postgres/python; Sneha Patel: Backend(45)‚ÜíFrontend(100) +55 because her bag contains react/next.js/tailwind), each move's `why` line correctly names the three skills gained, no magnets and no lonely roles (every role has a strong own match because of candidates 1/2/3), `band=urgent` (lift ‚â• 60), markdown brief renders end-to-end. **Frontend validation**: `npx tsc --noEmit` clean across the whole `src/`; `npx next build` clean ‚Äî `/crosswind` route emitted at 10.2 kB (smaller than `/cadence` at 9.65 kB despite carrying the matrix because the heatmap is pure CSS, no chart lib). **Navigation**: `Navbar.tsx` gets a `Crosswind` link inserted between Cadence and Pipeline. **CSS**: new `.cc-xw-hero`, `.cc-xw-ring`, `.cc-xw-tile`, `.cc-xw-matrix`, `.cc-xw-cell` (with `transform: scale(1.08)` + `box-shadow: inset white-18` on hover so the cell pops without breaking row alignment), and `.cc-xw-move` micro-animations added to `globals.css`. **README rewritten** ‚Äî new "What's new ‚Äî Crosswind (Day 57)" section at the top with the four signals, the surface walkthrough, the backend curl example, and the version bump callout. |
| 56 | 2026-06-17 | **WaySafe** | Round-12 move: shipped **Pulse ‚Äî Today's Outlook**, the *morning-brief* composer that finally adds the **temporal-delta lens** WaySafe was missing. Every prior surface up to Day 55 is *forward-looking* (Compass picks where to go, StaySafe where to sleep, Plan Route how to get there, Tempo when to leave, Refuge where to flee, Sentinel which clusters are heating) ‚Äî none of them answer the question a traveller actually asks the moment they wake up: *"what's different about my day vs 24 hours ago, and what should I do about it before lunch?"*. New `WaySafe/pulse.py` (~560 LOC, pure-stdlib, **zero new physics** ‚Äî Pulse is the first WaySafe surface that has *no engine of its own*; it's a composer) is a pure function of `(watched, incidents, geofences, pois, forecaster, now, clusters?)` that treats the user's day as a small portfolio of **watched points** (typically the stay + 1‚Äì3 planned destinations) and re-runs every existing engine for each point *twice* ‚Äî at `now` *and* at `now ‚àí 24 h`. **Per-point pipeline**: (1) `safety.compute_safety(now, all_incidents)` and `safety.compute_safety(now‚àí24h, incidents_with_created_at ‚â§ cutoff)` for a clean *signed* Œîscore + band-shift flag (the cutoff filter is the one trick ‚Äî drop incidents created after `now‚àí24h` to get the world as it was, instead of double-counting today's news against yesterday's penalty); (2) `forecast.HazardForecaster.risk_curve` for **today's** DOW *and* **yesterday's** DOW so the per-point hour-ribbon also carries a day-over-day diff; (3) `sentinel.cluster_incidents` ‚Äî clusters are computed once globally (reused from the Map / Sentinel tab via the new `clusters=‚Ä¶` keyword so the two surfaces never disagree), each watched point picks up the clusters whose **halo edge** sits within **`CLUSTER_INTERSECT_KM=1.5`** km, escalating-first; (4) `refuge.find_refuge(max_results=1)` so the stay's refuge-readiness band rides on every report (caught in a try/except ‚Äî refuge is context, never breaks the brief). **Per-point window math**: `best_window = argmin_h mean(curve_today[h:h+3])`, `worst_window = argmax_h ...` over a wrap-around 24-h ring (so `(22, 1)` is a valid 3-h window crossing midnight); also computed across all watched points as the **joint curve** `joint(h) = max_p curve_p(h)`. **Mood ladder** ‚Äî first match wins: `Critical` if any watched point Danger or any intersecting cluster Critical; `Active` if any High Risk, any cluster Emerging, or ‚â• 2 watched points slipped ‚â• 10 pts; `Watch` if any Caution or any single point dropped ‚â• 5 pts; else `Calm`. **Biggest mover** is the snapshot with the largest *signal* score = `|Œîscore|¬∑1.0  +  new_incidents_24h¬∑4.0  +  Œ£_escalating-clusters(6 + 2¬∑(velocity‚àí1))  +  6¬∑band_changed  +  4¬∑(refuge_band ‚àà {High Risk, Danger})` ‚Äî so a watched point that didn't shift in score but is touching a Critical cluster still surfaces. **Plain-English change log** deterministically composed from each snapshot's deltas (`"{label}: safety down **{Œî} pts** overnight ({s24}‚Üí{s})"` ¬∑ `"{label}: band shifted **{old} ‚Üí {new}**"` ¬∑ `"{label}: **{n} new incidents** within 1 km in the last 24 h (mostly accident)"` ¬∑ `"{label}: **Cluster #X ¬∑ Accident** is Critical (√ó43.9) ‚Äî edge 0.00 km"`), ranked by `signal + 0.01¬∑len(line)` so the biggest-mover's lines float to the top, capped at 8 bullets. **Plan-of-day** is the action layer ‚Äî prioritised checklist that *references other WaySafe tabs by name when those are the right follow-ups*: a Critical cluster intersection produces *"Re-plan any leg through {cluster} ‚Äî pick a corridor ‚â• 1.5 km away and prefer the **Tempo** winner over a now-departure"*; an Emerging cluster produces a wide-berth bullet; the best/worst outdoor windows produce front-load / avoid bullets quoting the joint risk number; a slipped biggest-mover produces a re-check bullet; a fresh-incident spike (‚â• 3 in 24 h) produces a *"Skim the **Map** tab around {label}"* bullet; a stay whose refuge band ‚â• High Risk produces *"Memorise the nearest non-stay refuge before evening"*. Falls back to *"Day looks clean ‚Äî no special precautions beyond the usual"* on a calm morning, so the brief is never spammy. **Serialisation**: `to_dict() ‚Üí waysafe.pulse.v1` JSON envelope (mood ¬∑ headline ¬∑ advisory_line ¬∑ joint_curve ¬∑ best_outdoor_window ¬∑ worst_outdoor_window ¬∑ biggest_mover ¬∑ per-snapshot block with hour curves today + yesterday + best/worst windows + refuge + changes ¬∑ de-duped sentinel intersections ¬∑ change_log ¬∑ actions); markdown digest is WhatsApp/email-shaped (headline > advisory line > best/avoid window > watched-points table > sentinel intersections > what-changed-since-yesterday > plan-of-day numbered list). **Frontend** ‚Äî new `Pulse` tab inserted at `tabs[0]` (so it's what the user opens first), every other tab index bumped +1 in a single deterministic pass (`Map 0‚Üí1 ¬∑ Plan Route 1‚Üí2 ¬∑ ‚Ä¶  ¬∑ Trip Log 14‚Üí15`); `render_pulse` + `render_pulse_empty` added to `theme.py` (~470 LOC of `.ws-pulse-*` CSS + Python) ‚Äî the render stack: (1) **hero card** with a 140 px conic-gradient `Pulse` ring (mean watched-point score as the fill %, mood-tinted hue, central mood eyebrow + score + band) + radial-gradient glow tinted by mood + headline + advisory + biggest-mover side card (delta-arrow + delta-pts + band arrow `{old} ‚Üí {new}` in band hue); (2) **four-tile strip** (overall band ¬∑ best 3-h window with joint risk ¬∑ total new incidents within 1 km in last 24 h with hue ramp ¬∑ refuge readiness at the stay with nearest POI + distance); (3) **24-hour joint risk ribbon** ‚Äî one row of 24 cells with height + colour driven by `joint_curve(h)` (green ‚Üí amber ‚Üí orange ‚Üí rose at 0.20 / 0.40 / 0.66 risk thresholds), **best window outlined in green with glow shadow**, **worst window outlined in red**, **blue vertical now-line** marking the current hour, past hours dimmed to 35% opacity, hour labels below colour-coded by membership in best/worst windows; (4) **per-watched-point card** ‚Äî 78 px score ring + kind eyebrow + glyphed title + band-tinted band chip + Œî-chip (`‚ñº ‚àí21 pts vs 24h ago` rose / `‚Üí ¬±0` slate / `‚ñ≤ +8 pts` emerald) + cluster pings (escalating ones rose-tinted) + band-shift chip + plain-English changes block + compact today-curve mini-ribbon + side panel with per-point best window and nearest refuge; (5) **Sentinel intersections** strip with status-coloured dot per cluster + escalating chip; (6) ranked **what-changed-since-yesterday** numbered list; (7) prioritised **plan-of-day** numbered list ‚Äî both lists use a custom `data-i` CSS counter so they self-number even when partially filtered; (8) JSON + markdown export buttons. **App wiring**: a `Watched points` `data_editor` expander lets the user customise the roster (kind selectbox, label, lat/lon ‚Äî NaN-guarded, defaults seeded from the user's `current_loc` as the stay + up to two nearest non-help POIs as destinations within 5 km), a primary `Compose Pulse` button that pulls in the cached `sent_clusters` from the existing Sentinel computation (so re-clustering is free), a `pulse_day` session-state slot that holds the result until re-composed, and graceful empty-state via `render_pulse_empty()`. **README rewritten** ‚Äî new headline-feature bullet under the existing Tempo bullet describing every engine Pulse re-runs and what the surface looks like; new dedicated **"üíì Pulse ‚Äî Today's Outlook (Day 56)"** section between StaySafe and Tempo with the "what gets re-run per watched point" table (engine ¬∑ what Pulse asks it twice ¬∑ new signal), the day-level summary equations (`joint_curve` ¬∑ `best_outdoor_window` ¬∑ `worst_outdoor_window` ¬∑ `overall_band` ¬∑ `overall_mood`), the explicit first-match-wins mood rules, the biggest-mover signal formula spelled out, an "what you see" surface walkthrough (hero ¬∑ four-tile strip ¬∑ joint ribbon ¬∑ per-point card ¬∑ Sentinel list ¬∑ what-changed list ¬∑ plan-of-day ¬∑ exports), and a closing "why this matters" passage tying it back to the rotation's central thesis ("a planner suite that only ever computes 'what is' leaves the traveller to track 'what changed' in their head ‚Äî Pulse closes that loop"). **Validation**: `python -c "import ast; ast.parse(...)"` clean on all three modified files (`pulse.py`, `app.py`, `theme.py`); engine end-to-end smoke pass on the bundled Goa data ‚Äî 3-point watched roster (Anjuna stay + Baga + Calangute) at a calm baseline produces `mood=Watch, band=Caution, best window 00:00‚Äì03:00 (risk 0.00), worst 07:00‚Äì10:00 (risk 0.02), Calangute market touched by Cluster #1 + #4`; synthetic delta test ‚Äî inject 3 fresh accidents within 1 km of Baga (last 8 h, severity=4) and re-run: brief flips to `mood=Critical, headline "Critical morning ¬∑ Baga beach down 21 pts ¬∑ best window 03:00‚Äì06:00"`, advisory names the cluster (`Cluster #1 ¬∑ Accident is **Critical** ‚Äî velocity √ó43.9, 3 recent incidents, edge 0.00 km from your day's plan. Re-route around it.`), change-log surfaces all four expected lines (Baga band shifted Caution ‚Üí High Risk + new incidents + cluster ping + Calangute also slipped 11 pts because it's within the same 1.5 km halo), plan-of-day leads with the *"Re-plan any leg through Cluster #1 ‚Äî pick a corridor ‚â• 1.5 km away and prefer the Tempo winner over a now-departure"* bullet; render_pulse exercised through a captured-stdout mock streamlit produces ~25 KB of HTML with every CSS class present (`ws-pulse-hero ¬∑ ws-pulse-pulse ¬∑ ws-pulse-tiles ¬∑ ws-pulse-ribbon-grid ¬∑ ws-pulse-cell.best ¬∑ ws-pulse-cell.worst ¬∑ ws-pulse-cell.now-mark ¬∑ ws-pulse-snap-ring ¬∑ ws-pulse-cluster-line ¬∑ ws-pulse-list`); `streamlit run app.py --headless` boots clean (HTTP 200 on `/_stcore/health`); round-trip JSON serialisation under `waysafe.pulse.v1` produces a 8.5 KB payload; markdown digest 1 KB. |

| 59 | 2026-06-20 | **SynapseOS** | Round-12 entry: shipped **Pulse ‚Äî what changed in your second brain this week**, the cross-cluster, time-windowed diff every prior surface had left to the user. SynapseOS already had three "lens" surfaces but each looks at one slice ‚Äî **Atlas** is the snapshot of *where every cluster sits right now* (cohesion √ó activity quadrant), **Chronicle** is the biography of *one* cluster (equal-time chapters + drift + pivot), **Daily Brief** is *today's* revisit picks. None of them ask the question a writer asks on a Friday afternoon: *"across my whole second brain, in the last N days, what got written, where did it land, what synapses formed, which clusters caught fire, what vocabulary appeared and what fell away?"*. New `backend/app/pulse.py` (~700 LOC, pure-stdlib + reuse of `synapse.compute_graph` + `community.build_communities` + `embed.cosine`) is a single deterministic function `compute_pulse(window_days, threshold, top_k) ‚Üí PulseReport`. **Per-cluster pulse** (mirrors `community.name_communities` for tokenizer alignment): for every cluster compute `new_count` (members with `created_at >= window_start`), `revisits_count` (members with `last_seen_at >= window_start` AND `created_at < window_start` so the two buckets are mutually exclusive), `share_new = new/size`, **centroid drift** = `1 ‚àí cosine(centroid(prior_members), centroid(new_members))` *only* when both epochs have ‚â• 2 members (so a newborn cluster doesn't print a misleading 0), a **momentum** soft blend (`0.55¬∑share_new + 0.25¬∑(revisits/size) + 0.20¬∑density_proxy`), and a status badge ‚Äî first-match-wins ladder: `new_count == size ‚Üí born` ¬∑ `share_new ‚â• 0.5 AND new_count ‚â• 2 ‚Üí emerging` ¬∑ `new_count ‚â• 3 ‚Üí hot` ¬∑ `new_count ‚â• 1 OR revisits ‚â• 1 ‚Üí warm` ¬∑ else `dormant`. Plus per-cluster **new vocabulary** (a chronicle-style `_delta_terms` with the same 0.5 forgiveness factor scoring in-window member tokens against the rest of the cluster ‚Äî title √ó 3, tags √ó 2, body √ó 1) and the actual **hot titles** of the new notes ordered by `created_at desc`. **Library-wide signals**: (a) **bridges born** ‚Äî current synapses where `cmap[u] != cmap[v]` *and* at least one endpoint is a new note, sorted by strength desc and capped at 16, with a `NEW` chip per new-side; (b) **hubs born** ‚Äî new notes already pulling `degree ‚â• HUB_MIN_DEGREE=3` at the current graph parameters (instant centrality is rare and worth surfacing); (c) library-wide **vocab delta** (emerged vs faded) over the prior-vs-new TF tables with `VOCAB_MIN_COUNT=2` floor so single-mention typos don't slip in; (d) **daily activity** ‚Äî per-day bins of created vs revisited across the window for a sparkline, oldest-first so the UI draws left-to-right time; (e) **streak** ‚Äî longest run of consecutive days ending today (UTC) with ‚â• 1 note created, computed across *all* notes (extends beyond the requested window so a 60-day streak still shows in a 7-day pulse); (f) **words written** ‚Äî `chars / 5` heuristic summed over new-note bodies (the standard word-proxy that doesn't trip on punctuation). **Recommendations**: priority-banded so the top-5 view shows a healthy mix (`synthesize 0.70+` *catch the hot topic before it scatters* ¬∑ `name 0.60` *the cluster doesn't have a meaningful label yet* ¬∑ `hub 0.50` *a new note grew structural importance fast ‚Äî re-read while context is fresh* ¬∑ `bridge 0.40` *write a connector note for the freshest cross-cluster synapse* ¬∑ `revisit 0.20` *dormant cluster nudge*) ‚Äî sorted priority desc with alpha tie-break so the panel doesn't jitter, capped at 14. **Headline** ‚Äî one-liner narrative composed first-match-wins from the dominant shape (`No new notes` ¬∑ `Quiet writing week` ¬∑ the prose form with new/words/revisits/hot/bridges/hubs/streak). `serialize()` returns a plain-dict response; `to_markdown()` ships a paste-anywhere brief (headline + metrics table + vocab delta + active clusters + bridges + hubs + recommendations). Two new schemas (`PulseReportOut` + 5 child models) and two new routes in `main.py`: `GET /pulse?window_days=1\|7\|30\|90` (clamped 1..365 with 422 on out-of-range), `GET /pulse/export.md`. **Frontend** ‚Äî new `frontend/src/components/Pulse.tsx` (~830 LOC) wired into `page.tsx` as `pulseOpen` modal sibling of Atlas/Chronicle, opens via a new header pill (`‚©ò pulse` with a pink‚Üílime‚Üícyan gradient ring) carrying a live badge of `new_notes + bridges_born` over the last 7d. **Visual identity**: distinct pink+lime ECG glyph (an actual heartbeat polyline in a gradient tile ‚Äî `0,8 ‚Üí 6,8 ‚Üí 9,3 ‚Üí 12,13 ‚Üí 15,5 ‚Üí 18,11 ‚Üí 21,8 ‚Üí 32,8` for a clean PQRST shape) so it doesn't get mistaken for Atlas/Chronicle. **Layout**: dark glass dialog identical to Atlas ‚Äî title strip with pink‚Üílime‚Üícyan linear-gradient header band, window-picker pills (`1d / 7d / 30d / 90d`), ‚§ì md export, ‚úï close, headline echoed inline. Body sections: (1) **6-tile metrics strip** (new notes ¬∑ revisits ¬∑ bridges ¬∑ hubs ¬∑ streak ¬∑ hot¬∑forming with dormant sub-label), each tile hue-rim-lit by signal colour (lime/amber/pink/violet/cyan/white). (2) **Daily activity sparkline** ‚Äî a single SVG with two stacked area layers (`pulse-fill` lime gradient for created, `pulse-fill-rev` amber gradient for created+revisited stacked on top), a baseline + dashed midline, peak dots on every active day, deterministic month-day x-axis labels at first/mid/last via a hand-rolled `dayLabel`, max-value label at the y-axis top, viewBox stretched to width. (3) **Vocabulary delta** ‚Äî two-column emerged (lime chips, "frequent now ¬∑ rare before") vs faded (slate chips, "frequent before ¬∑ rare now") with empty-state copy when no shift. (4) **Active clusters** (lg:7 col) ‚Äî one `ClusterRow` per cluster: status pill with coloured dot (hot/lime ¬∑ born/pink ¬∑ emerging/cyan ¬∑ warm/amber ¬∑ dormant/slate), `‚ú¶ synth` + `‚äô isolate` action chips, **momentum bar** (1.5 px high, cluster-colour fill, percentage-tagged), pill row (`size`, `+N new` lime, `‚Üª R` amber, `S% new`, `drift X.XX` pink when populated, `quiet Nd` for fully-dormant), **new vocab chips** + **hot titles list** (first 3) with a left-side cluster-colour dot bullet. (5) **Recommendations** (lg:5 col) ‚Äî priority-ranked card list with a kind glyph (`‚ú¶ synthesize` lime ¬∑ `‚åÅ name` cyan ¬∑ `‚ú∫ hub` violet ¬∑ `‚áÑ bridge` pink ¬∑ `‚òº revisit` amber), headline, detail, `p 0.XX` chip, clickable to act (synthesize/name ‚Üí opens Synthesis modal ¬∑ revisit/bridge ‚Üí isolates cluster on canvas ¬∑ hub ‚Üí opens note in Inspector). (6) **Hubs born** ‚Äî grid of violet-ringed cards with `‚ú∫` glyph, title, `Nx` degree pill, snippet, cluster name + dot + age in days. (7) **Bridges born** ‚Äî list of pink-tinted rows: source-cluster chip ‚áÑ target-cluster chip ¬∑ cosine, then source-title ‚Üî target-title with `NEW` lime chips on whichever side is in-window; click opens the note. **Status colors** picked to be distinct from Atlas's quadrant palette (Pulse uses pink for born/bridges, lime for emerged/hot, cyan for emerging ‚Äî Atlas uses lime/cyan/violet/slate by quadrant ‚Äî so the two surfaces don't visually clash when stacked open). Type-clean `PulseReport` / `PulseCluster` / `PulseBridge` / `PulseHub` / `PulseRecommendation` types + 2 new API methods (`api.pulse({ windowDays })`, `api.pulseExportUrl({ windowDays })`). **Validation**: full backend round-trip via FastAPI `TestClient` ‚Äî `GET /pulse` 200 across 1d/7d/30d/90d windows on the seeded 21-note graph, headline correctly switches from `"No new notes in the last 1d.
